It was said: O Messenger of God, not even the angels? He said: "Not even the angels. The angels are compelled, like the sun and the moon." This is a hadith that is extremely gharib (singular, rarely narrated).

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ تَشْرِيفِهِ لِبَنِي آدَمَ، وَتَكْرِيمِهِ إِيَّاهُمْ، فِي خَلْقِهِ لَهُمْ عَلَى أَحْسَنِ الْهَيْئَاتِ وَأَكْمَلِهَا كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿لَقَدْ خَلَقْنَا الإنْسَانَ فِي أَحْسَنِ تَقْوِيمٍ﴾ [التِّينِ: ٤] أَيْ: يَمْشِي قَائِمًا مُنْتَصِبًا عَلَى رِجْلَيْهِ، وَيَأْكُلُ بِيَدَيْهِ -وَغَيْرُهُ مِنَ الْحَيَوَانَاتِ يَمْشِي عَلَى أَرْبَعٍ وَيَأْكُلُ بِفَمِهِ -وَجَعَلَ لَهُ سَمْعًا وَبَصَرًا وَفُؤَادًا، يَفْقَهُ بِذَلِكَ كُلِّهِ وَيَنْتَفِعُ بِهِ، وَيُفَرِّقُ بَيْنَ الْأَشْيَاءِ، وَيَعْرِفُ مَنَافِعَهَا وَخَوَاصَّهَا وَمَضَارَّهَا فِي الْأُمُورِ الدُّنْيَوِيَّةِ وَالدِّينِيَّةِ.

﴿وَحَمَلْنَاهُمْ فِي الْبَرِّ﴾ أَيْ: عَلَى الدَّوَابِّ مِنَ الْأَنْعَامِ وَالْخَيْلِ وَالْبِغَالِ، وَفِي "الْبَحْرِ" أَيْضًا عَلَى السُّفُنِ الْكِبَارِ وَالصِّغَارِ.

﴿وَرَزَقْنَاهُمْ مِنَ الطَّيِّبَاتِ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ زُرُوعٍ وَثِمَارٍ، وَلُحُومٍ وَأَلْبَانٍ، مِنْ سَائِرِ أَنْوَاعِ الطُّعُومِ وَالْأَلْوَانِ، الْمُشْتَهَاةِ اللَّذِيذَةِ، وَالْمَنَاظِرِ الْحَسَنَةِ، وَالْمَلَابِسِ الرَّفِيعَةِ مِنْ سَائِرِ الْأَنْوَاعِ، عَلَى اخْتِلَافِ أَصْنَافِهَا وَأَلْوَانِهَا وَأَشْكَالِهَا، مِمَّا يَصْنَعُونَهُ لِأَنْفُسِهِمْ، وَيَجْلِبُهُ إِلَيْهِمْ غَيْرُهُمْ مِنْ أَقْطَارِ الْأَقَالِيمِ وَالنَّوَاحِي.

﴿وَفَضَّلْنَاهُمْ عَلَى كَثِيرٍ مِمَّنْ خَلَقْنَا تَفْضِيلا﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ سَائِرِ الْحَيَوَانَاتِ وَأَصْنَافِ الْمَخْلُوقَاتِ.

وَقَدِ استُدل بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ عَلَى أَفْضَلِيَّةِ جِنْسِ الْبَشَرِ عَلَى جِنْسِ الْمَلَائِكَةِ، قَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: أَخْبَرَنَا مَعْمَر، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ قَالَ: قَالَتِ الْمَلَائِكَةُ: يَا رَبَّنَا، إِنَّكَ أَعْطَيْتَ بَنِي آدَمَ الدُّنْيَا، يَأْكُلُونَ مِنْهَا وَيَتَنَعَّمُونَ، وَلَمْ تُعْطِنَا ذَلِكَ فَأَعْطِنَاهُ فِي الْآخِرَةِ. فَقَالَ اللَّهُ: "وَعِزَّتِي وَجَلَالِي لَا أَجْعَلُ صَالِحَ ذُرِّيَّةِ مَنْ خَلَقْتُ بِيَدِي، كَمَنْ قُلْتُ لَهُ: كُنْ فَكَانَ" .

وَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ مُرْسَلٌ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ، وَقَدْ رُوِيَ مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ مُتَّصِلًا.

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو الْقَاسِمِ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ محمد بن صَدَقَة البغدادي، حدثنا إبراهيم بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ خَالِدٍ المِصِّيصِيّ، حَدَّثَنَا حَجَّاجُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو غَسَّان مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ مُطَرِّفٍ، عَنْ صَفْوَانَ بْنِ سُليم، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ يَسَارٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ الْمَلَائِكَةَ قَالَتْ: يَا رَبَّنَا، أَعْطَيْتَ بَنِي آدَمَ الدُّنْيَا، يَأْكُلُونَ فِيهَا وَيَشْرَبُونَ وَيَلْبَسُونَ، وَنَحْنُ نُسَبِّحُ بِحَمْدِكَ وَلَا نَأْكُلُ وَلَا نَشْرَبُ وَلَا نَلْهُو، فَكَمَا جَعَلْتَ لَهُمُ الدُّنْيَا فَاجْعَلْ لَنَا الْآخِرَةَ. قَالَ: لَا أَجْعَلُ صَالِحَ ذُرِّيَّةِ مَنْ خَلَقْتُ بِيَدِي، كَمَنْ قُلْتُ لَهُ: كُنْ، فَكَانَ" .

وَقَدْ رَوَى ابْنُ عَسَاكِرَ مِنْ طَرِيقِ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ أَيُّوبَ الرَّازِيِّ، حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ بْنُ عَلِيِّ بْنِ خَلَفٍ الصَّيْدَلَانِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، حَدَّثَنِي عُثْمَانُ بْنُ حِصْنِ بْنِ عُبَيْدَةَ بْنِ عَلاق، سَمِعْتُ عُرْوَةَ بْنَ رُوَيْم اللَّخْمِيَّ، حَدَّثَنِي أَنَسُ بْنُ مَالِكٍ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ الْمَلَائِكَةَ قَالُوا: رَبَّنَا، خَلَقْتَنَا وَخَلَقْتَ بَنِي آدَمَ، فَجَعَلْتَهُمْ يَأْكُلُونَ الطَّعَامَ، وَيَشْرَبُونَ الشَّرَابَ، وَيَلْبَسُونَ الثِّيَابَ، وَيَتَزَوَّجُونَ النِّسَاءَ، وَيَرْكَبُونَ الدَّوَابَّ، يَنَامُونَ وَيَسْتَرِيحُونَ، وَلَمْ تَجْعَلْ لَنَا مِنْ ذَلِكَ شَيْئًا، فَاجْعَلْ لَهُمُ الدُّنْيَا وَلَنَا الْآخِرَةَ. فَقَالَ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: لَا أَجْعَلُ مَنْ خَلَقْتُهُ بِيَدِي، وَنَفَخْتُ فِيهِ مِنْ رُوحِي، كَمَنْ قُلْتُ لَهُ: كُنْ، فَكَانَ" .

وَقَالَ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدَانُ بْنُ أَحْمَدَ، حَدَّثَنَا عُمَرُ بْنُ سَهْلٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عُبَيْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ تَمَّامٍ، عَنْ خَالِدٍ الْحَذَاءِ، عَنْ بِشْرِ بْنِ شِغَاف عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَا شَيْءٌ أَكْرَمُ عَلَى اللَّهِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ مِنَ ابْنِ آدَمَ". قِيلَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ وَلَا الْمَلَائِكَةُ؟ قَالَ: "وَلَا الْمَلَائِكَةُ، الْمَلَائِكَةُ مَجْبُورُونَ بِمَنْزِلَةِ الشَّمْسِ وَالْقَمَرِ" . وَهَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ جِدًّا.

---

## 17:71-72 — verses 71-72 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, blessed and exalted, informs about the Day of Resurrection: that He will hold every community to account by their imam.

They have differed concerning this. Mujahid and Qatadah said: meaning by their prophet. This is like His saying: {And for every community there is a messenger. So when their messenger comes, judgment will be rendered between them in justice, and they will not be wronged} [Yunus: 47].

Some of the salaf said: this is the greatest honor for the people of hadith, because their imam is the Prophet ﷺ.

Ibn Zayd said: by their book which was revealed to their prophet, containing the legislation.

Ibn Jarir chose this view. It has been related from Ibn Abi Najih, from Mujahid, that he said: by their books. It is possible that he meant this, or that he meant what al-Awfi related from Ibn Abbas concerning His saying: {The Day We call every people by their imam}, meaning: by the book of their deeds. Abu al-Aliyah, al-Hasan, and al-Dahhak said likewise. This view is the preferred one, because of His saying, exalted is He: {And everything We have enumerated in a clear register (imam)} [Ya-Sin: 12]. And He, exalted is He, said: {And the record will be placed, and you will see the criminals fearful of what is in it, and they will say: Woe to us, what is this record that leaves nothing small or great without having enumerated it? And they will find what they did present, and your Lord does not wrong anyone} [al-Kahf: 49].

And He, exalted is He, said: {And you will see every community kneeling. Every community will be called to its record. Today you will be recompensed for what you used to do. This is Our record which speaks concerning you in truth. Indeed We used to record what you were doing} [al-Jathiyah: 28-29].

This does not contradict the fact that the prophet will be brought when God judges between his community, for he must inevitably be a witness against it regarding its deeds, as He said: {And the earth will shine with the light of its Lord, and the record will be placed, and the prophets and the witnesses will be brought} [al-Zumar: 69], and He said: {How will it be when We bring from every community a witness, and We bring you as a witness over these} [al-Nisa: 41].

But what is meant here by imam is the record of deeds. This is why He, exalted is He, said: {The Day We call every people by their imam. Then whoever is given his record in his right hand, those will read their record}, meaning: out of his joy and delight at the righteous deeds contained in it, he reads it and loves reading it, as He, exalted is He, said: {As for one who is given his record in his right hand, he will say: Here, read my record! Indeed I was certain that I would meet my account} up to His saying: {But as for one who is given his record in his left hand, he will say: Would that I had not been given my record, and had not known what my account was} [al-Haqqah: 19-26].

Regarding His saying: {and they will not be wronged a fatil (thread)}, it has already been mentioned that the fatil is the elongated thread found in the crease of a date pit.

The hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bazzar related a hadith concerning this, saying: [chain] Muhammad ibn Ya'mar and Muhammad ibn Uthman ibn Karamah said, Ubaydullah ibn Musa narrated to us, from Isra'il, from al-Suddi, from his father, from Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with him, from the Prophet ﷺ, concerning God's saying: {The Day We call every people by their imam}, he said: "One of them will be called and given his record in his right hand, and his body will be extended for him, and his face will be whitened, and a crown of pearl will be placed upon his head, gleaming. He will then go to his companions and they will see him from afar, and they will say: O God, bring this one to us, and bless us in this one. So he will come to them and say to them: Rejoice, for each man among you will have the like of this. As for the disbeliever, his face will be blackened, and his body will be extended for him, and his companions will see him and say: We seek refuge in God from this, or: from the evil of this. O God, do not bring him to us. So he will come to them and they will say: O God, disgrace him. And he will say: May God distance you, for each man among you will have the like of this."

Then al-Bazzar said: it is not related except by this route.

Regarding His saying: {And whoever is blind in this [world] will be blind in the Hereafter, and further astray from the path}, Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, Qatadah, and Ibn Zayd said: {And whoever is in this} meaning in the worldly life {blind} to the proofs of God, His signs, and His clear evidences, {will be in the Hereafter blind} meaning he will remain so, {and further astray from the path}, meaning more astray than he was, as he was in this world. We seek refuge in God from that.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى عَنْ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ: أَنَّهُ يُحَاسِبُ كُلَّ أُمَّةٍ بِإِمَامِهِمْ.

وَقَدِ اخْتَلَفُوا فِي ذَلِكَ، فَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ وَقَتَادَةُ: أَيْ بِنَبِيِّهِمْ. وَهَذَا كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلِكُلِّ أُمَّةٍ رَسُولٌ فَإِذَا جَاءَ رَسُولُهُمْ قُضِيَ بَيْنَهُمْ بِالْقِسْطِ وَهُمْ لَا يُظْلَمُونَ﴾ [يُونُسَ: ٤٧] .

وَقَالَ بَعْضُ السَّلَفِ: هَذَا أَكْبَرُ شَرَفٍ لِأَصْحَابِ الْحَدِيثِ؛ لِأَنَّ إِمَامَهُمُ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ زَيْدٍ: بِكِتَابِهِمُ الَّذِي أُنْزِلَ عَلَى نَبِيِّهِمْ، مِنَ التَّشْرِيعِ.

وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَرُوِيَ عَنِ ابْنِ أَبِي نَجِيح، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: بِكُتُبِهِمْ. فَيُحْتَمَلُ أَنْ يَكُونَ أَرَادَ هَذَا، وَأَنْ يَكُونَ أَرَادَ مَا رَوَاهُ الْعَوْفِيُّ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿يَوْمَ نَدْعُو كُلَّ أُنَاسٍ بِإِمَامِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: بِكِتَابِ أَعْمَالِهِمْ، وَكَذَا قَالَ أَبُو الْعَالِيَةِ، وَالْحَسَنُ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ. وَهَذَا الْقَوْلُ هُوَ الْأَرْجَحُ؛ لِقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَكُلَّ شَيْءٍ أحْصَيْنَاهُ فِي إِمَامٍ مُبِينٍ﴾ [يس: ١٢] . وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَوُضِعَ الْكِتَابُ فَتَرَى الْمُجْرِمِينَ مُشْفِقِينَ مِمَّا فِيهِ وَيَقُولُونَ يَا وَيْلَتَنَا مَالِ هَذَا الْكِتَابِ لَا يُغَادِرُ صَغِيرَةً وَلا كَبِيرَةً إِلا أَحْصَاهَا وَوَجَدُوا مَا عَمِلُوا حَاضِرًا وَلا يَظْلِمُ رَبُّكَ أَحَدًا﴾ [الْكَهْفِ: ٤٩] .

وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَتَرَى كُلَّ أُمَّةٍ جَاثِيَةً كُلُّ أُمَّةٍ تُدْعَى إِلَى كِتَابِهَا الْيَوْمَ تُجْزَوْنَ مَا كُنْتُمْ تَعْمَلُونَ هَذَا كِتَابُنَا يَنْطِقُ عَلَيْكُمْ بِالْحَقِّ إِنَّا كُنَّا نَسْتَنْسِخُ مَا كُنْتُمْ تَعْمَلُونَ﴾ [الْجَاثِيَةِ: ٢٨، ٢٩] .

وَهَذَا لَا يُنَافِي أَنْ يُجَاءَ بِالنَّبِيِّ إِذَا حَكَمَ اللَّهُ بَيْنَ أُمَّتِهِ، فَإِنَّهُ لَا بُدَّ أَنْ يَكُونَ شَاهِدًا عَلَيْهَا بِأَعْمَالِهَا، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَأَشْرَقَتِ الأرْضُ بِنُورِ رَبِّهَا وَوُضِعَ الْكِتَابُ وَجِيءَ بِالنَّبِيِّينَ وَالشُّهَدَاءِ﴾ [الزُّمَرِ: ٦٩] ، وَقَالَ ﴿فَكَيْفَ إِذَا جِئْنَا مِنْ كُلِّ أُمَّةٍ بِشَهِيدٍ وَجِئْنَا بِكَ عَلَى هَؤُلاءِ شَهِيدًا﴾ [النِّسَاءِ: ٤١] ..

وَلَكِنَّ الْمُرَادَ هَاهُنَا بِالْإِمَامِ هُوَ كِتَابُ الْأَعْمَالِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَ نَدْعُو كُلَّ أُنَاسٍ بِإِمَامِهِمْ فَمَنْ أُوتِيَ كِتَابَهُ بِيَمِينِهِ فَأُولَئِكَ يَقْرَءُونَ كِتَابَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ فَرْحَتِهِ وَسُرُورِهِ بِمَا فِيهِ مِنَ الْعَمَلِ الصَّالِحِ، يَقْرَؤُهُ وَيُحِبُّ قِرَاءَتَهُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَأَمَّا مَنْ أُوتِيَ كِتَابَهُ بِيَمِينِهِ فَيَقُولُ هَاؤُمُ اقْرَءُوا كِتَابِيَهْ إِنِّي ظَنَنْتُ أَنِّي مُلاقٍ حِسَابِيَهْ﴾ إِلَى أَنْ قَالَ: ﴿وَأَمَّا مَنْ أُوتِيَ كِتَابَهُ بِشِمَالِهِ فَيَقُولُ يَا لَيْتَنِي لَمْ أُوتَ كِتَابِيَهْ وَلَمْ أَدْرِ مَا حِسَابِيَهْ﴾ [الْحَاقَّةِ: ١٩ -٢٦] ..

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلا يُظْلَمُونَ فَتِيلا﴾ قَدْ تَقَدَّمَ أَنَّ "الْفَتِيلَ" هُوَ الْخَيْطُ الْمُسْتَطِيلُ فِي شِقِّ النَّوَاةِ.

وَقَدْ رَوَى الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَزَّارُ حَدِيثًا فِي هَذَا فَقَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ يَعْمَر وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عُثْمَانَ بْنِ كَرَامَةَ قَالَا حَدَّثَنَا عُبَيْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ مُوسَى، عَنْ إِسْرَائِيلَ، عَنِ السُّدِّيّ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ في قول الله: ﴿يَوْمَ نَدْعُو كُلَّ أُنَاسٍ بِإِمَامِهِمْ﴾ قَالَ: "يُدْعَى أَحَدُهُمْ فَيُعْطَى كِتَابَهُ بِيَمِينِهِ، وَيُمَدُّ لَهُ فِي جِسْمِهِ، ويُبَيَّض وَجْهُهُ، وَيُجْعَلُ عَلَى رَأْسِهِ تَاجٌ مِنْ لؤْلؤة تَتَلألأ فَيَنْطَلِقُ إِلَى أَصْحَابِهِ فَيَرَوْنَهُ مِنْ بَعِيدٍ، فَيَقُولُونَ: اللَّهُمَّ ائْتِنَا بِهَذَا، وَبَارِكْ لَنَا فِي هَذَا. فَيَأْتِيهِمْ فَيَقُولُ لَهُمْ: أَبْشِرُوا، فَإِنَّ لِكُلِّ رَجُلٍ مِنْكُمْ مِثْلَ هَذَا. وَأَمَّا الْكَافِرُ فَيُسْود وَجْهُهُ، وَيُمَدُّ لَهُ فِي جِسْمِهِ، وَيَرَاهُ أَصْحَابُهُ فَيَقُولُونَ: نَعُوذُ بِاللَّهِ مِنْ هَذَا -أَوْ: مِنْ شَرِّ هَذَا -اللَّهُمَّ لَا تَأْتِنَا بِهِ. فَيَأْتِيهِمْ فَيَقُولُونَ: اللَّهُمَّ أَخْزِهِ فَيَقُولُ: أَبْعَدَكُمُ اللَّهُ، فَإِنَّ لكل رجل منكم مثل هذا".

ثُمَّ قَالَ الْبَزَّارُ: لَا يُرْوَى إِلَّا مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَنْ كَانَ فِي هَذِهِ أَعْمَى فَهُوَ فِي الآخِرَةِ أَعْمَى وَأَضَلُّ سَبِيلا﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَابْنُ زَيْدٍ: ﴿وَمَنْ كَانَ فِي هَذِهِ﴾ أَيْ: فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا ﴿أَعْمَى﴾ عَنْ حُجَجِ اللَّهِ وَآيَاتِهِ وَبَيِّنَاتِهِ ﴿فَهُوَ فِي الآخِرَةِ أَعْمَى﴾ أَيْ: كَذَلِكَ يَكُونُ ﴿وَأَضَلُّ سَبِيلا﴾ أَيْ: وَأَضَلُّ مِنْهُ كَمَا كَانَ فِي الدُّنْيَا، عِيَاذًا بِاللَّهِ مِنْ ذَلِكَ.

---

## 17:73-75 — verses 73-75 (shared commentary)

### Translation

God Most High informs us of His support for His Messenger ﷺ, of His establishing him firmly, and of His protecting and preserving him from the evil of evildoers and the plotting of the wicked. He, Most High, is the One who takes charge of his affair and his victory, and He does not entrust him to any of His creatures. Rather, He is his protector, his guardian, his helper, his supporter, and the one who grants him triumph, the one who makes his religion prevail over whoever showed him enmity, opposed him, or contended against him, in the easts of the earth and its wests, ﷺ, with abundant peace, until the Day of Judgment.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ تَأْيِيدِ رَسُولِهِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ وَسَلَامُهُ ، وَتَثْبِيتِهِ، وَعِصْمَتِهِ وَسَلَامَتِهِ مِنْ شَرِّ الْأَشْرَارِ وَكَيْدِ الْفُجَّارِ، وَأَنَّهُ تَعَالَى هُوَ الْمُتَوَلِّي أَمْرَهُ وَنَصْرَهُ، وَأَنَّهُ لَا يَكِلُهُ إِلَى أَحَدٍ مِنْ خَلْقِهِ، بَلْ هُوَ وَلِيُّهُ وَحَافِظُهُ وَنَاصِرُهُ وَمُؤَيِّدُهُ وَمُظَفِّرُهُ، وَمُظْهِرُ دِينَهُ عَلَى مَنْ عَادَاهُ وَخَالَفَهُ وَنَاوَأَهُ، فِي مَشَارِقِ الْأَرْضِ وَمَغَارِبِهَا، ﷺ تَسْلِيمًا كَثِيرًا إِلَى يَوْمِ الدِّينِ.

---

## 17:76-77 — verses 76-77 (shared commentary)

### Translation

It has been said that this was revealed concerning the Jews, when they suggested to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ that he should reside in Sham, the land of the prophets, and abandon residence in Medina.

This view is weak, because this verse is Meccan, and residence in Medina came after that.

It has also been said that it was revealed at Tabuk. But there is doubt about the soundness of this.

Al-Bayhaqi said, from al-Hakim, from al-Asamm, from Ahmad ibn Abd al-Jabbar al-Utaridi, from Yunus ibn Bukayr, from Abd al-Hamid ibn Bahram, from Shahr ibn Hawshab, from Abd al-Rahman ibn Ghanm: that the Jews came to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ one day and said, "O Abu al-Qasim, if you are truthful that you are a prophet, then go to Sham, for Sham is the land of the gathering and the land of the prophets." He believed what they said, and so he set out on the expedition of Tabuk, intending nothing but Sham. When he reached Tabuk, Allah sent down to him verses from Surat Bani Isra'il after the surah had already been sealed: {And indeed, they were about to drive you out from the land to expel you from it} up to His saying: {a transferal}. So Allah commanded him to return to Medina, and said, "In it is your life and your death, and from it you will be resurrected."

There is doubt concerning this chain of transmission. The more apparent view is that this is not sound, for the Prophet ﷺ did not campaign at Tabuk because of what the Jews said. Rather, he campaigned there in compliance with His saying, Exalted is He: {O you who believe, fight those of the disbelievers who are near to you} [al-Tawbah: 123], and His saying, Exalted is He: {Fight those who do not believe in Allah nor in the Last Day, and who do not forbid what Allah and His Messenger have forbidden, and do not follow the religion of truth, from among those who were given the Scripture, until they pay the jizyah willingly while they are humbled} [al-Tawbah: 29]. He campaigned there to retaliate and avenge those of his Companions who had been killed at Mu'tah, and Allah knows best. And if this report were sound, the hadith narrated by al-Walid ibn Muslim, from Ufayr ibn Ma'dan, from Sulaym ibn Amir, from Abu Umamah, may Allah be pleased with him, would be understood in light of it. He said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "The Qur'an was sent down in three places: Mecca, Medina, and Sham." Al-Walid said: meaning Bayt al-Maqdis (Jerusalem). Interpreting "Sham" here as Tabuk is better than what al-Walid said, that it means Bayt al-Maqdis, and Allah knows best.

It has also been said that it was revealed concerning the disbelievers of Quraysh, when they intended to drive the Messenger out from among them. Allah threatened them with this verse, saying that if they drove him out, they would remain in Mecca after him only a little while. And that is indeed what happened, for after his emigration from among them, once their harm to him had intensified, they remained only a year and a half, until Allah brought them together with him at Badr without any prior appointment. He gave him power over them and made him victorious over them, so he killed their nobles and took their chiefs captive. Hence He said: {The way of those We sent before you of Our messengers} meaning, this is Our way regarding those who disbelieved in Our messengers and harmed them: the messenger is driven out from among them, and then punishment comes to them. Were it not that he, peace and blessings be upon him, is the Messenger of Mercy, punishments would have come upon them in this world that no one could withstand. Hence Allah, Exalted is He, said: {And Allah would not punish them while you are among them, nor would Allah punish them while they seek forgiveness} [al-Anfal: 33].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قِيلَ: نَزَلَتْ فِي الْيَهُودِ، إِذْ أَشَارُوا عَلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِسُكْنَى الشَّامِ بِلَادِ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ، وَتَرْكِ سُكْنَى الْمَدِينَةِ.

وَهَذَا الْقَوْلُ ضَعِيفٌ؛ لِأَنَّ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ مَكِّيَّةٌ، وَسُكْنَى الْمَدِينَةِ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ.

وَقِيلَ: إِنَّهَا نَزَلَتْ بِتَبُوكَ. وَفِي صِحَّتِهِ نَظَرٌ.

قَالَ الْبَيْهَقِيُّ، عَنِ الْحَاكِمُ، عَنِ الْأَصَمِّ، عَنْ أَحْمَدَ بْنِ عَبْدِ الْجَبَّارِ العُطاردي، عَنْ يُونُسُ بْنُ بُكيْر، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْحَمِيدِ بْنِ بَهْرَام، عَنْ شَهْر بْنِ حَوْشَب، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ غَنْم؛ أَنَّ الْيَهُودَ أَتَوْا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَوْمًا فَقَالُوا: يَا أَبَا الْقَاسِمِ، إِنْ كُنْتَ صَادِقًا أَنَّكَ نَبِيٌّ، فَالْحَقْ بِالشَّامِ؛ فَإِنَّ الشَّامَ أَرْضُ الْمَحْشَرِ وَأَرْضُ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ. فَصَدَّقَ مَا قَالُوا، فَغَزَا غَزْوَةَ تَبُوكَ، لَا يُرِيدُ إِلَّا الشَّامَ. فَلَمَّا بَلَغَ تَبُوكَ، أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ آيَاتٍ مِنْ سُورَةِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ بَعْدَ مَا خُتِمَتِ السُّورَةُ: ﴿وَإِنْ كَادُوا لَيَسْتَفِزُّونَكَ مِنَ الأرْضِ لِيُخْرِجُوكَ مِنْهَا﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿تَحْوِيلا﴾ فَأَمَرَهُ اللَّهُ بِالرُّجُوعِ إِلَى الْمَدِينَةِ، وَقَالَ: فِيهَا محياك ومماتك، ومنها تبعث .

وَفِي هَذَا الْإِسْنَادِ نَظَرٌ. وَالْأَظْهَرُ أَنَّ هَذَا لَيْسَ بِصَحِيحٍ؛ فَإِنَّ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ لَمْ يَغْزُ تَبُوكَ عَنْ قَوْلِ الْيَهُودِ، إِنَّمَا غَزَاهَا امْتِثَالًا لِقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا قَاتِلُوا الَّذِينَ يَلُونَكُمْ مِنَ الْكُفَّارِ﴾ [التَّوْبَةِ: ١٢٣] ، وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿قَاتِلُوا الَّذِينَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ بِاللَّهِ وَلا بِالْيَوْمِ الآخِرِ وَلا يُحَرِّمُونَ مَا حَرَّمَ اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ وَلا يَدِينُونَ دِينَ الْحَقِّ مِنَ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ حَتَّى يُعْطُوا الْجِزْيَةَ عَنْ يَدٍ وَهُمْ صَاغِرُونَ﴾ [التَّوْبَةِ: ٢٩] . وَغَزَاهَا لِيَقْتَصَّ وَيَنْتَقِمَ مِمَّنْ قَتَلَ أَهْلَ مُؤْتَةَ، مِنْ أَصْحَابِهِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ. وَلَوْ صَحَّ هَذَا لَحُمِلَ عَلَيْهِ الْحَدِيثُ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ الْوَلِيدُ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ عُفَير بْنِ مَعْدَانَ، عَنْ سُلَيم بْنِ عَامِرٍ، عَنْ أَبِي أُمَامَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أُنْزِلَ الْقُرْآنُ فِي ثَلَاثَةِ أَمْكِنَةٍ: مَكَّةَ، وَالْمَدِينَةِ، وَالشَّامِ" . قَالَ الْوَلِيدُ: يَعْنِي بَيْتَ الْمَقْدِسِ. وَتَفْسِيرُ الشَّامِ بِتَبُوكَ أَحْسَنُ مِمَّا قَالَ الْوَلِيدُ: إِنَّهُ بَيْتُ الْمَقْدِسِ وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقِيلَ: نَزَلَتْ فِي كَفَّارِ قُرَيْشٍ، هَمُّوا بِإِخْرَاجِ الرَّسُولِ مِنْ بَيْنِ أَظْهُرِهِمْ، فَتَوَعَّدَهُمُ اللَّهُ بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ، وَأَنَّهُمْ لَوْ أَخْرَجُوهُ لَمَا لَبِثُوا بَعْدَهُ بِمَكَّةَ إِلَّا يَسِيرًا. وَكَذَلِكَ وَقَعَ؛ فَإِنَّهُ لَمْ يَكُنْ بَعْدَ هِجْرَتِهِ مِنْ بَيْنِ أَظْهُرِهِمْ، بَعْدَ مَا اشْتَدَّ أَذَاهُمْ لَهُ، إِلَّا سَنَةٌ وَنِصْفٌ. حَتَّى جَمَعَهُمُ اللَّهُ وَإِيَّاهُ بِبَدْرٍ عَلَى غَيْرِ مِيعَادٍ، فَأَمْكَنَهُ مِنْهُمْ وَسَلَّطَهُ عَلَيْهِمْ وَأَظْفَرَهُ بِهِمْ، فَقَتَلَ أَشْرَافَهُمْ وَسَبَى سَرَاتَهُمْ ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿سُنَّةَ مَنْ قَدْ أَرْسَلْنَا قَبْلَكَ مِنْ رُسُلِنَا﴾ أَيْ: هَكَذَا عَادَتُنَا فِي الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا بِرُسُلِنَا وَآذَوْهُمْ: يَخْرُجُ الرَّسُولُ مِنْ بَيْنِ أَظْهُرِهِمْ: وَيَأْتِيهِمُ الْعَذَابُ. وَلَوْلَا أَنَّهُ عَلَيْهِ [الصَّلَاةُ وَ] السَّلَامُ رَسُولُ الرَّحْمَةِ، لَجَاءَهُمْ مِنَ النِّقَمِ فِي الدُّنْيَا مَا لَا قِبَلَ لِأَحَدٍ بِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ لِيُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَأَنْتَ فِيهِمْ وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ مُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَهُمْ يَسْتَغْفِرُونَ﴾ [الْأَنْفَالِ: ٣٣] .

---

## 17:78-79 — verses 78-79 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says to His Messenger ﷺ, commanding him to establish the prescribed prayers at their appointed times: {Establish prayer at the decline of the sun}. It has been said this means at its setting. This was said by Ibn Mas'ud, Mujahid, and Ibn Zayd.

Hushaym said, from Mughirah, from al-Sha'bi, from Ibn Abbas: "its decline" means its zenith passing (zawal). This was also narrated by Nafi', from Ibn Umar. Malik narrated it in his Tafsir, from al-Zuhri, from Ibn Umar. Abu Barzah al-Aslami said the same, and it is also a report from Ibn Mas'ud and Mujahid. Al-Hasan, al-Dahhak, Abu Ja'far al-Baqir, and Qatadah said likewise. Ibn Jarir chose this view, and among the evidence he cited for it is what he narrated from Ibn Humayd, from al-Hakam ibn Bashir: "Amr ibn Qays narrated to us, from Ibn Abi Layla, [from a man], from Jabir ibn Abd Allah, who said: I invited the Messenger of Allah ﷺ and whoever he wished among his companions, and they ate at my house. Then they went out when the sun had passed its zenith. The Prophet ﷺ went out and said: 'Come out, O Abu Bakr, for this is the time when the sun has declined (dalakat).'"

He then narrated it from Sahl ibn Bakkar, from Abu Awanah, from al-Aswad ibn Qays, from Nubayh al-Anazi, from Jabir, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, in similar wording. According to this, this verse would encompass the times of all five prayers: from His saying {at the decline of the sun} to {the darkness of night}, which is its blackness (though it has also been said to mean the setting of the sun), from which the times of Zuhr, Asr, Maghrib, and Isha are derived. And His saying [the Almighty]: {and the Qur'an of dawn} means the dawn prayer (Fajr).

The Sunnah has been established from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ through mass-transmitted reports (tawatur), from his actions and sayings, detailing these times, in accordance with what the people of Islam practice today, which they received generation after generation, one century after another, as is established in its proper place. Praise be to Allah.

{Indeed, the Qur'an of dawn is witnessed}. Al-A'mash said, from Ibrahim, from Ibn Mas'ud, and from Abu Salih, from Abu Hurayrah, may Allah be pleased with him, from the Prophet ﷺ, regarding this verse {Indeed, the Qur'an of dawn is witnessed}, that he said: "It is witnessed by the angels of the night and the angels of the day."

Al-Bukhari said: Abd Allah ibn Muhammad narrated to us, Abd al-Razzaq narrated to us, Ma'mar informed us, from al-Zuhri, from Abu Salamah and Sa'id ibn al-Musayyib, from Abu Hurayrah, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "The prayer performed in congregation exceeds the prayer of one person alone by twenty-five degrees, and the angels of the night and the angels of the day gather together at the dawn prayer." Abu Hurayrah says: Recite if you wish: {and the Qur'an of dawn, indeed the Qur'an of dawn is witnessed}.

Imam Ahmad said: Asbat narrated to us, al-A'mash narrated to us, from Ibrahim, from Ibn Mas'ud, from the Prophet ﷺ, and al-A'mash also narrated to us, from Abu Salih, from Abu Hurayrah, from the Prophet ﷺ, concerning His saying {and the Qur'an of dawn, indeed the Qur'an of dawn is witnessed}, that he said: "It is witnessed by the angels of the night and the angels of the day."

Al-Tirmidhi, al-Nasa'i, and Ibn Majah all narrated it, the three of them from Ubayd ibn Asbat ibn Muhammad, from his father, with the same chain. Al-Tirmidhi said: hasan sahih (good and authentic).

In a wording found in the two Sahihs, by way of Malik, from Abu al-Zinad, from al-A'raj, from Abu Hurayrah, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "The angels of the night and the angels of the day take turns among you, and they meet together at the dawn prayer and at the afternoon prayer. Then those who spent the night among you ascend, and He asks them, though He knows best about you, 'How did you leave My servants?' They say: 'We came to them while they were praying, and we left them while they were praying.'" Abd Allah ibn Mas'ud said: The two guards meet at the dawn prayer, and these ascend while those take their place.

Ibrahim al-Nakha'i, Mujahid, Qatadah, and others said the same in explaining this verse.

As for the hadith which Ibn Jarir narrated here, from the hadith of al-Layth ibn Sa'd, from Ziyadah, from Muhammad ibn Ka'b al-Qurazi, from Fadalah ibn Ubayd, from Abu al-Darda, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, he mentioned the hadith of the Descent (al-Nuzul), and that the Almighty says: "Whoever asks My forgiveness, I will forgive him. Whoever asks Me, I will give him. Whoever calls upon Me, I will answer him, until dawn breaks." For this reason He says {and the Qur'an of dawn, indeed the Qur'an of dawn is witnessed}, meaning Allah witnesses it, as do the angels of the night and the angels of the day. Ziyadah is alone in narrating this, and he has a hadith on this matter in the Sunan of Abu Dawud.

His saying {And in part of the night, perform tahajjud with it, as a supererogatory act for you} is a command to him to perform night prayer after the obligatory prayer, as reported in Sahih Muslim, from Abu Hurayrah, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he was asked: "Which prayer is most excellent after the obligatory prayer?" He said: "The prayer of the night."

For this reason the Almighty commanded His Messenger, after the obligatory prayers, to perform night prayer, for tahajjud is that which occurs after sleep. This was said by Alqamah, al-Aswad, Ibrahim al-Nakha'i, and others, and it is the well-known meaning in the language of the Arabs. Likewise, hadiths have been established from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ that he used to perform tahajjud after his sleep, narrated from Ibn Abbas, A'ishah, and others among the Companions, may Allah be pleased with them, as is elaborated in its proper place. Praise and gratitude be to Allah.

Al-Hasan al-Basri said: it is that which occurs after the Isha prayer. But this should be understood as referring to what comes after sleep.

There is disagreement over the meaning of His saying {as a supererogatory act for you}. It has been said that its meaning is that you alone are singled out for the obligation of this, thereby making night prayer obligatory upon him specifically, but not upon the community (ummah). This was narrated by al-Awfi from Ibn Abbas, and it is one of two views held by the scholars, and one of two views of al-Shafi'i, may Allah have mercy on him, and Ibn Jarir chose it.

It has also been said that night prayer was made a supererogatory act specifically in his case because he had already been forgiven for what preceded of his sin and what would come after, whereas others of his ummah have their supererogatory prayers expiate for the sins that are upon them. This was said by Mujahid, and it is found in the Musnad, from Abu Umamah al-Bahili, may Allah be pleased with him.

His saying {It may be that your Lord will raise you to a praiseworthy station} means: do this which I have commanded you, so that We may raise you on the Day of Resurrection to a station which all creation and their Creator, blessed and exalted is He, will envy you for.

Ibn Jarir said: most of the people of interpretation said: that is the station in which he ﷺ will stand on the Day of Resurrection to intercede for the people, so that their Lord may relieve them from the great distress they are in on account of the severity of that day.

Mention of those who said this: Ibn Bashshar narrated to us, Abd al-Rahman narrated to us, Sufyan narrated to us, from Abu Ishaq, from Silah ibn Zufar, from Hudhayfah, who said: The people will be gathered on a single plain, where the caller can make himself heard by all of them and the eye can see all of them, barefoot and naked, as they were created, standing, and no soul will speak except by His permission. It will be called out: "O Muhammad!" And he will say: "Here I am, at Your service, and good is in Your hands, and evil is not attributed to You, and whoever is rightly guided is guided by You, and Your servant stands before You, and by You and to You, there is no escape and no refuge from You except to You. Blessed and exalted are You, glory be to You, Lord of the House." This is the Praiseworthy Station (al-maqam al-mahmud) which Allah, mighty and majestic, has mentioned.

He then narrated it from Bundar, from Ghundar, from Shu'bah, from Abu Ishaq, with the same chain. Abd al-Razzaq likewise narrated it from Ma'mar and al-Thawri, from Abu Ishaq, with the same chain.

Ibn Abbas said: this Praiseworthy Station is the station of intercession. Ibn Abi Najih said the same, from Mujahid. Al-Hasan al-Basri said likewise.

Qatadah said: he is the first for whom the earth will split open, and the first intercessor, and the people of knowledge held the view that this is the Praiseworthy Station which Allah mentioned: {It may be that your Lord will raise you to a praiseworthy station}.

I say: for the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, upon whom be peace, there are honors [on the Day of Resurrection] in which no one shares with him, and honors in which no one equals him. He is the first for whom the earth will split open, and he will be raised riding to the place of gathering. He holds the banner (liwa) under which Adam and all who come after him will stand. He has the pool (hawd) at which more people will come to drink than at any other place in the standing ground. He has the greatest intercession before Allah, whereby he will come forward for the final judgment between the creatures, and that is after the people ask Adam, then Noah, then Abraham, then Moses, then Jesus, each of them saying: "I am not fit for it," until they come to Muhammad ﷺ, who will say: "I am fit for it, I am fit for it," as we shall mention in detail in this place, if Allah the Almighty wills. Among this is that he will intercede for peoples who have been ordered to the Fire, and they will be turned back from it. He is the first of the prophets for whose community judgment will be rendered, and the first of them to be permitted to cross the Sirat with his community. He is the first intercessor in Paradise, as is established in Sahih Muslim.

And in the hadith of the Trumpet: all the believers will not enter Paradise except through his intercession, and he is the first one to enter it, and his nation before all other nations. He will be permitted to intercede for the raising of the ranks of peoples whose deeds do not reach that level. He is the possessor of al-Wasilah (the Means, the highest rank in Paradise), which befits no one but him. When Allah, Exalted is He, permits intercession for the sinners, the angels, the prophets, and the believers will intercede, and he will intercede for created beings whose number none knows but Allah. No one will intercede as he does, nor will anyone equal him in that. I have already gone into this in detail at the end of the book "al-Sirah," in the chapter on the special distinctions [of the Prophet ﷺ], and to Allah belongs praise and grace.

Let us now mention the hadiths that have come down concerning the Praiseworthy Station, and Allah is the one whose help is sought:

Al-Bukhari said: [chain] ... I heard Ibn Umar saying: On the Day of Resurrection, people will become kneeling groups, each nation following its prophet. They will say: "O so-and-so, intercede! O so-and-so, intercede!" until the intercession reaches the Prophet ﷺ. That is the day when Allah will raise him to a Praiseworthy Station.

It was also narrated by Hamzah ibn Abdullah, from his father, from the Prophet ﷺ.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] ... I heard Hamzah ibn Abdullah ibn Umar say: I heard Abdullah ibn Umar say: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The sun will draw near until the sweat reaches halfway up the ear. While they are in that state, they will seek help from Adam, and he will say: 'I am not fit for that.' Then from Musa, and he will say the same. Then from Muhammad, and he will intercede between the created beings. He will walk until he takes hold of the ring of the door of Paradise. On that day Allah will raise him to a Praiseworthy Station." [The people of Paradise will all praise him for it.]

Al-Bukhari narrated it likewise in "al-Zakah" from Yahya ibn Bukayr and Abdullah ibn Salih, both from al-Layth ibn Sa'd, with the same chain, and he added: "On that day Allah will raise him to a Praiseworthy Station, for which all the people gathered will praise him."

Al-Bukhari said: [chain] ... from Jabir ibn Abdullah, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Whoever, upon hearing the call to prayer, says: 'O Allah, Lord of this perfect call and of the established prayer, grant Muhammad al-Wasilah and al-Fadilah, and raise him to the Praiseworthy Station which You have promised him,' my intercession will become permissible for him on the Day of Resurrection." Al-Bukhari alone narrated this, not Muslim.

The hadith of Ubayy:

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] ... from al-Tufayl ibn Ubayy ibn Ka'b, from his father, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "When the Day of Resurrection comes, I will be the leader of the prophets and their speaker, and the possessor of their intercession, without boasting."

Al-Tirmidhi reported it from the hadith of Abu Amir Abd al-Malik ibn Amr al-Aqadi, and said: "Hasan sahih (sound, good)." Ibn Majah reported it from the hadith of Abdullah ibn Muhammad ibn Aqil with the same chain. We have already mentioned earlier, in the hadith of Ubayy ibn Ka'b concerning the recitation of the Qur'an according to seven letters, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said at its end: "I said: 'O Allah, forgive my nation. O Allah, forgive my nation,' and I delayed the third supplication for a day when all creation will turn to me in longing, even Ibrahim (peace be upon him)."

The hadith of Anas ibn Malik:

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] ... from Anas, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "The believers will gather on the Day of Resurrection, and it will be inspired in them to say: 'If only we sought intercession with our Lord, that He might relieve us from this place of ours.' So they will come to Adam and say: 'O Adam, you are the father of mankind. Allah created you with His hand, made His angels prostrate to you, and taught you the names of all things. So intercede for us with your Lord, that He may relieve us from this place of ours.' Adam will say to them: 'I am not fit for that,' and he will mention the sin he committed, and he will feel shame before his Lord, Mighty and Majestic, because of it. He will say: 'But go to Nuh, for he was the first messenger Allah sent to the people of the earth.' So they will come to Nuh, and he will say: 'I am not fit for that,' and he will mention his fault of asking his Lord for that of which he had no knowledge, and he will feel shame before his Lord because of it. 'But go to Ibrahim, the intimate friend of the Most Merciful.' So they will come to him, and he will say: 'I am not fit for that. But go to Musa, a servant to whom Allah spoke directly and to whom He gave the Torah.' So they will come to Musa, and he will say: 'I am not fit for that,' and he will mention to them the soul he killed without right, and he will feel shame before his Lord because of it. 'But go to Isa, the servant of Allah and His messenger, His word and a spirit from Him.' So they will come to Isa, and he will say: 'I am not fit for that. But go to Muhammad, a servant whose past and future sins have been forgiven.' So they will come to me." Al-Hasan said this phrase: "So I will rise and walk between two rows of the believers." Anas said: "Until I seek permission before my Lord. When I see my Lord, I will fall down, or I will collapse, prostrating before my Lord. He will leave me thus as long as Allah wills to leave me." He said: "Then it will be said: 'Raise your head, O Muhammad. Speak, and you will be heard. Intercede, and your intercession will be accepted. Ask, and you will be given.' So I will raise my head and praise Him with a praise that He will teach me. Then I will intercede, and He will set a limit for me, and I will admit them into Paradise." "Then I will return to Him a second time. When I see my Lord, I will fall down, or I will collapse, prostrating before my Lord. He will leave me thus as long as Allah wills to leave me. Then it will be said: 'Raise your head, O Muhammad. Speak, and you will be heard. Ask, and you will be given. Intercede, and your intercession will be accepted.' So I will raise my head and praise Him with a praise that He will teach me. Then I will intercede, and He will set a limit for me, and I will admit them into Paradise. Then I will return a third time. When I see my Lord, I will fall down, or I will collapse, prostrating before my Lord. He will leave me thus as long as Allah wills to leave me. Then it will be said: 'Raise your head, O Muhammad. Speak, and you will be heard. Ask, and you will be given. Intercede, and your intercession will be accepted.' So I will raise my head and praise Him with a praise that He will teach me. Then I will intercede, and He will set a limit for me, and I will admit them into Paradise. Then I will return a fourth time and say: 'O my Lord, none remains except those held back by the Qur'an.'" Anas ibn Malik related to us that the Prophet ﷺ said: "Then whoever said 'There is no god but Allah' and had in his heart good equal to the weight of a grain of barley will come out of the Fire. Then whoever said 'There is no god but Allah' and had in his heart good equal to the weight of a grain of wheat will come out of the Fire. Then whoever said 'There is no god but Allah' and had in his heart good equal to the weight of an atom will come out of the Fire."

Both [al-Bukhari and Muslim] narrated it [in the Sahih] from the hadith of Sa'id, with the same chain. Imam Ahmad likewise narrated it from Affan, from Hammad ibn Salamah, from Thabit, from Anas, in its full length.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] ... from al-Nadr ibn Anas, from Anas, who said: The Prophet of Allah ﷺ told me: "I was standing, waiting for my nation to cross the Bridge, when Isa (peace be upon him) came to me and said: 'These are the prophets who have come to you, O Muhammad, asking' or he said 'gathering to you, and calling upon Allah to separate all the nations, to wherever Allah wills, because of the distress they are in.' The people will be bridled by their sweat. As for the believer, it will be upon him like a slight cold, but as for the disbeliever, death will overtake him." He said: "Wait until I return to you." So the Prophet of Allah ﷺ went and stood beneath the Throne, and he encountered what no chosen angel nor sent prophet had ever encountered. Allah, Mighty and Majestic, revealed to Jibril: "Go to Muhammad and say to him: 'Raise your head, ask and you will be given, intercede and your intercession will be accepted.'" "So I interceded for my nation, that one person out of every ninety-nine be brought out. I kept returning again and again to my Lord, Mighty and Majestic, and I did not stand before Him in any station without being granted intercession, until Allah gave me from that, saying: 'O Muhammad, admit from your nation, from among Allah's creation, whoever bore witness that there is no god but Allah sincerely, even for a single day, and died upon that.'"

The hadith of Buraydah, may Allah be pleased with him:

Imam Ahmad ibn Hanbal said: [chain] ... from Ibn Buraydah, from his father: that he entered upon Mu'awiyah, and there was a man speaking. Buraydah said: "O Mu'awiyah, will you permit me to speak?" He said, "Yes," thinking that he would say something similar to what the other man had said. Buraydah said: I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "I hope to intercede on the Day of Resurrection for a number equal to every tree and clod of earth upon the earth."

He said: "Then do you hope for it, O Mu'awiyah, while Ali, may Allah be pleased with him, does not hope for it?!"

The hadith of Ibn Mas'ud:

Imam Ahmad said: Arim ibn al-Fadl narrated to us, Sa'id ibn Zayd narrated to us, Ali ibn al-Hakam al-Bunani narrated to us, from Uthman, from Ibrahim, from Alqamah and al-Aswad, from Ibn Mas'ud, who said: The two sons of Mulaykah came to the Prophet ﷺ and said, "Our mother used to honor her husband and show compassion to her children," and he mentioned that she also honored the guest, "except that she had buried a daughter alive in the Jahiliyyah (pre-Islamic era)." He said, "Your mother is in the Fire." They turned away with distress visible on their faces, so he ordered them called back, and they returned, with joy visible on their faces, hoping that something new had been revealed. He said, "My mother is with your mother." A man among the hypocrites said, "That does not benefit his mother at all, and we tread in his footsteps!" Then a man from the Ansar, and I have never seen a man who asked more questions than him, said, "O Messenger of Allah, has your Lord promised you concerning it or concerning them?" He thought the man was asking about something he had heard of, so he said, "Whatever Allah my Lord wills, and what He has made me hope for, I shall indeed stand in al-Maqam al-Mahmud (the Praised Station) on the Day of Resurrection." The man from the Ansar said, "O Messenger of Allah, what is that Praised Station?" He said, "That is when you will be brought forth barefoot, naked, uncircumcised. The first to be clothed will be Ibrahim (peace be upon him), who will say, 'Clothe My friend.' Two white garments will be brought, and he will wear them, then he will be seated facing the Throne. Then my garment will be brought to me and I will wear it, and I will stand at His right in a station that no one else will occupy, which the first and the last will envy me for. And a river from al-Kawthar will be opened flowing to the Basin." The hypocrites said, "Water has never flowed except over stony ground or pebbles." The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "Its stony ground is musk, and its pebbles are pearls." [The hypocrite said, "I have never heard anything like today. It is rare that water flows over stony ground or pebbles without there being vegetation for it." The Ansari said, "O Messenger of Allah, does it have vegetation?" He said, "Yes, branches of gold."] The hypocrite said, "I have never heard anything like today, for it is rare that a branch grows without putting forth leaves, and without bearing fruit!" The Ansari said, "O Messenger of Allah, does it have fruit?" He said, "Yes, of the colors of gems, and its water is whiter than milk and sweeter than honey. Whoever drinks one drink of it will never thirst again, and whoever is deprived of it will never be satisfied afterward."

Abu Dawud al-Tayalisi said: Yahya ibn Salamah ibn Kuhayl narrated to us, from his father, from Abu al-Za'ra, from Abdullah, who said: Then Allah, Mighty and Majestic, will permit intercession, and the Holy Spirit, Jibril, will stand up, then Ibrahim, the Friend of Allah, will stand up, then Isa or Musa will stand up, Abu al-Za'ra said, "I do not know which of the two," he said, then your Prophet ﷺ will stand up fourth, and he will intercede, and no one after him will intercede more than he intercedes, and this is al-Maqam al-Mahmud which Allah, Mighty and Majestic, mentioned: {It may be that your Lord will raise you to a Praised Station}.

The hadith of Ka'b ibn Malik, may Allah be pleased with him:

Imam Ahmad said: Yazid ibn Abd Rabbih narrated to us, Muhammad ibn Harb narrated to us, al-Zubaydi narrated to us, from al-Zuhri, from Abd al-Rahman ibn Abdullah ibn Ka'b ibn Malik, from Ka'b ibn Malik, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "The people will be resurrected on the Day of Resurrection, and I and my nation will be upon a hillock, and my Lord, Mighty and Majestic, will clothe me in a green garment. Then I will be given permission, and I will say what Allah wills me to say, and that is al-Maqam al-Mahmud."

The hadith of Abu al-Darda, may Allah be pleased with him:

Imam Ahmad said: Hasan narrated to us, Ibn Lahi'ah narrated to us, Yazid ibn Abi Habib narrated to us, from Abd al-Rahman ibn Jubayr, from Abu al-Darda, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "I am the first for whom permission will be given to prostrate on the Day of Resurrection, and I am the first for whom permission will be given to raise his head. I will look at what is in front of me and recognize my nation from among all the nations, and likewise behind me, and likewise on my right, and likewise on my left." A man said, "O Messenger of Allah, how will you recognize your nation from among the nations, given all those between Nuh and your nation?" He said, "They will be bright of face and limb, from the traces of wudu, no one else will be like that. And I will recognize them in that they will be given their records in their right hands, and I will recognize them in that their offspring will run before them."

The hadith of Abu Hurayrah, may Allah be pleased with him:

Imam Ahmad, may Allah have mercy on him, said: Yahya ibn Sa'id narrated to us, Abu Hayyan narrated to us, Abu Zur'ah ibn Amr ibn Jarir narrated to us, from Abu Hurayrah, who said: Meat was brought to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and the foreleg was raised up to him, for he loved it. He took a bite from it, then said, "I am the master of mankind on the Day of Resurrection. Do you know why that is? Allah will gather the first and the last on one plain, so that a caller will make them all hear and the eye will encompass all of them, and the sun will draw near, so that people will experience distress and anguish that they cannot bear or endure. So some people will say to others, [Do you not see the state you are in? Do you not see what has befallen you? Will you not look for someone to intercede for you with your Lord, Mighty and Majestic?] So some people will say to others: 'Your father Adam!'

So they will come to Adam and say, 'O Adam, you are the father of mankind. Allah created you with His own hand and breathed into you of His spirit, and commanded the angels, and they prostrated to you. So intercede for us with your Lord. Do you not see the state we are in? Do you not see what has befallen us?' Adam will say, 'My Lord has become angry today with an anger the like of which He has never been angry before, and will never be angry with the like of it again. He forbade me from the tree, and I disobeyed Him. Myself, myself, myself! Go to someone other than me, go to Nuh.'

So they will come to Nuh and say, 'O Nuh, you are the first of the messengers to the people of the earth, and Allah named you a grateful servant. Intercede for us with your Lord. Do you not see the state we are in? Do you not see what has befallen us?' Nuh will say, 'My Lord has become angry today with an anger the like of which He has never been angry before, and will never be angry with the like of it again. I had a supplication against my people. Myself, myself, myself! Go to someone other than me, go to Ibrahim.'

So they will come to Ibrahim and say, 'O Ibrahim, you are the prophet of Allah and His friend from among the people of the earth, [intercede for us with your Lord]. Do you not see the state we are in? Do you not see what has befallen us?' He will say, 'My Lord has become angry today with an anger the like of which He has never been angry before, and will never be angry with the like of it again,' and he will mention his lies. 'Myself, myself, myself! [Go to someone other than me,] go to Musa.'

So they will come to Musa and say, 'O Musa, you are the messenger of Allah. Allah chose you with His messages and with His speech above mankind. Intercede for us with your Lord. Do you not see the state we are in? Do you not see what has befallen us?' Musa will say to them, 'My Lord has become angry today with an anger the like of which He has never been angry before, and will never be angry with the like of it again. I killed a person whom I was not commanded to kill. Myself, myself, myself! Go to someone other than me, go to Isa.'

So they will come to Isa and say, 'O Isa, you are the messenger of Allah and His word which He cast unto Maryam, and a spirit from Him,' he said, that is how it is, 'and you spoke to people from the cradle. So intercede for us with your Lord. Do you not see the state we are in? Do you not see what has befallen us?' Isa will say to them, 'My Lord has become angry today with an anger the like of which He has never been angry before, and will never be angry with the like of it again,' and he did not mention a sin, 'Go to someone other than me, go to Muhammad.'

So they will come to me and say, 'O Muhammad, you are the messenger of Allah and the seal of the prophets. Allah has forgiven you your past and future sins. So intercede for us with your Lord. Do you not see the state we are in? Do you not see what has befallen us?' So I will rise and go beneath the Throne, and fall down in prostration before my Lord, Mighty and Majestic. Then Allah will open unto me and inspire me with praises of Him and beautiful commendation of Him such as He has not opened to anyone before me. Then it will be said, 'O Muhammad, raise your head, ask and you shall be given, intercede and your intercession shall be accepted.' So I will say, 'O Lord, my nation, my nation! O Lord, my nation, my nation! O Lord, my nation, my nation!' Then it will be said, 'O Muhammad, admit those of your nation who are not subject to reckoning through the right gate of the gates of Paradise, and they shall share with the rest of the people in the other gates besides it.'" Then he said, "By the One in whose hand is the soul of Muhammad, the space between the two leaves of one of the doors of Paradise is like the distance between Makkah and Hajar, or like the distance between Makkah and Busra." Both of them (al-Bukhari and Muslim) reported it in their Sahihs.

Muslim, may God have mercy on him, said: Al-Hakam ibn Musa narrated to us, Hiql ibn Ziyad narrated to us, from al-Awza'i, Abu 'Ammar narrated to me, 'Abdullah ibn Farrukh narrated to me, Abu Hurayrah narrated to me, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "I am the master of the children of Adam on the Day of Resurrection, the first for whom the grave will split open, the first intercessor, and the first whose intercession will be accepted."

Ibn Jarir said: Abu Kurayb narrated to us, Waki' narrated to us, from Dawud ibn Yazid al-Za'afiri, from his father, from Abu Hurayrah, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said, concerning {It may be that your Lord will raise you to a praiseworthy station}: he was asked about it, and he said: "It is the intercession."

Imam Ahmad related it from Waki' and from Muhammad ibn 'Ubayd, from Dawud, from his father, from Abu Hurayrah, from the Prophet ﷺ, concerning the words of the Most High {It may be that your Lord will raise you to a praiseworthy station}, who said: "It is the station in which I will intercede for my nation."

'Abd al-Razzaq said: Ma'mar informed us, from al-Zuhri, from 'Ali ibn al-Husayn, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "When the Day of Resurrection comes, God will stretch out the earth as one stretches a hide, until there is no space left for any human being except the space of his foot." The Prophet ﷺ said: "I will be the first to be called, with Gabriel on the right of the Most Merciful, and by God, he had never seen Him before that. I will say: 'My Lord, this one has informed me that You sent him to me.' God, blessed and exalted is He, will say: 'He has spoken the truth.' Then intercession will be granted to me, and I will say: 'My Lord, Your servants worshipped You in the far reaches of the earth.'" He said: "That is the praiseworthy station." This is a mursal (a report with a gap after the Companion) hadith.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى لِرَسُولِهِ ﷺ آمِرًا لَهُ بِإِقَامَةِ الصَّلَوَاتِ الْمَكْتُوبَاتِ فِي أَوْقَاتِهَا: ﴿أَقِمِ الصَّلاةَ لِدُلُوكِ الشَّمْسِ﴾ قِيلَ لِغُرُوبِهَا. قَالَهُ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَابْنُ زَيْدٍ.

وَقَالَ هُشَيْم، عَنْ مُغِيرَةَ، عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: "دُلُوكُهَا": زَوَالُهَا. وَرَوَاهُ نَافِعٌ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ. وَرَوَاهُ مَالِكٌ فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ. وَقَالَهُ أَبُو بَرْزَة الْأَسْلَمِيُّ وَهُوَ رِوَايَةٌ أَيْضًا عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ. وَمُجَاهِدٍ. وَبِهِ قَالَ الْحَسَنُ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَأَبُو جَعْفَرٍ الْبَاقِرُ، وَقَتَادَةُ. وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَمِمَّا اسْتُشْهِدَ عَلَيْهِ مَا رَوَاهُ عَنِ ابْنِ حُمَيْدٍ، عَنِ الْحَكَمِ بْنِ بَشِيرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَمْرُو بْنُ قَيْسٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ أَبِي لَيْلَى، [عَنْ رَجُلٍ] ، عَنِ جَابِرِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: دَعَوْتُ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَمَنْ شَاءَ مِنْ أَصْحَابِهِ فَطَعِمُوا عِنْدِي، ثُمَّ خَرَجُوا حِينَ زَالَتِ الشَّمْسُ، فَخَرَجَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ فَقَالَ: "اخْرُجْ يَا أَبَا بَكْرٍ، فَهَذَا حِينَ دلكت الشمس" .

ثُمَّ رَوَاهُ عَنْ سَهْلِ بْنِ بَكَّارٍ، عَنْ أَبِي عَوَانة، عَنِ الْأَسْوَدِ بْنِ قَيْسٍ، عَنْ نُبَيْحٍ الْعَنَزِيِّ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، نَحْوَهُ. فَعَلَى هَذَا تَكُونُ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ دَخَلَ فِيهَا أَوْقَاتُ الصَّلَاةِ الْخَمْسَةِ فَمِنْ قَوْلِهِ: ﴿لِدُلُوكِ الشَّمْسِ إِلَى غَسَقِ اللَّيْلِ﴾ وَهُوَ: ظَلَامُهُ، وَقِيلَ: غُرُوبُ الشَّمْسِ، أُخِذَ مِنْهُ الظُّهْرُ وَالْعَصْرُ وَالْمَغْرِبُ وَالْعَشَاءُ، وَقَوْلُهُ [تَعَالَى] : ﴿وَقُرْآنَ الْفَجْرِ﴾ يَعْنِي: صَلَاةَ الْفَجْرِ.

وَقَدْ ثَبَتَتِ السُّنَّةُ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ تَوَاتُرًا مِنْ أَفْعَالِهِ وَأَقْوَالِهِ بِتَفَاصِيلَ هَذِهِ الْأَوْقَاتِ، عَلَى مَا عَلَيْهِ عَمَلُ أَهْلِ الْإِسْلَامِ الْيَوْمَ، مِمَّا تَلَقَّوْهُ خَلَفًا عَنْ سَلَفٍ، وَقَرْنًا بَعْدَ قَرْنٍ، كَمَا هُوَ مُقَرَّرٌ فِي مَوَاضِعِهِ، وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ.

﴿إِنَّ قُرْآنَ الْفَجْرِ كَانَ مَشْهُودًا﴾ قَالَ الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ -وَعَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿إِنَّ قُرْآنَ الْفَجْرِ كَانَ مَشْهُودًا﴾ قَالَ: "تَشْهَدُهُ مَلَائِكَةُ اللَّيْلِ وَمَلَائِكَةُ النَّهَارِ" .

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، أَخْبَرَنَا مَعْمَر، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ -وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ الْمُسَيَّبِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "فَضْلُ صَلَاةِ الْجَمِيعِ عَلَى صَلَاةِ الْوَاحِدِ خَمْسٌ وَعِشْرُونَ دَرَجَةً، وَتَجْتَمِعُ مَلَائِكَةُ اللَّيْلِ وَمَلَائِكَةُ النَّهَارِ فِي صَلَاةِ الْفَجْرِ". وَيَقُولُ أَبُو هُرَيْرَةَ: اقْرَءُوا إِنْ شِئْتُمْ: ﴿وَقُرْآنَ الْفَجْرِ إِنَّ قُرْآنَ الْفَجْرِ كَانَ مَشْهُودًا﴾ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَسْبَاطٌ، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ -وَحَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَقُرْآنَ الْفَجْرِ إِنَّ قُرْآنَ الْفَجْرِ كَانَ مَشْهُودًا﴾ قَالَ: "تَشْهَدُهُ مَلَائِكَةُ اللَّيْلِ، وَمَلَائِكَةُ النَّهَارِ".

وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ، وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ، ثَلَاثَتُهُمْ عَنْ عُبَيْد بْنِ أَسْبَاطِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، بِهِ وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ.

وَفِي لَفْظٍ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ، مِنْ طَرِيقِ مَالِكٌ، عَنْ أَبِي الزِّناد، عَنِ الْأَعْرَجِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: " يَتَعَاقَبُونَ فِيكُمْ مَلَائِكَةُ اللَّيْلِ وَمَلَائِكَةُ النَّهَارِ ، وَيَجْتَمِعُونَ فِي صَلَاةِ الصُّبْحِ وَفِي صَلَاةِ الْعَصْرِ، فَيَعْرُجُ الَّذِينَ بَاتُوا فِيكُمْ فَيَسْأَلُهُمْ -وَهُوَ أَعْلَمُ بِكُمْ -كَيْفَ تَرَكْتُمْ عِبَادِي؟ فَيَقُولُونَ: أَتَيْنَاهُمْ وَهُمْ يُصَلُّونَ، وَتَرَكْنَاهُمْ وَهُمْ يُصَلُّونَ" وَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ مَسْعُودٍ: يَجْتَمِعُ الْحَرَسَانِ فِي صَلَاةِ الفجر، فيصعد هؤلاء ويقيم هؤلاء.

وَكَذَا قَالَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ النَّخَعي، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ فِي تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ.

وَأَمَّا الْحَدِيثُ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ هَاهُنَا -مِنْ حَدِيثِ اللَّيْثِ بْنِ سَعْدٍ، عَنْ زِيَادَةَ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ كَعْبٍ الْقُرَظِيِّ، عَنْ فَضَالَةَ بْنِ عُبيد، عَنْ أَبِي الدَّرْدَاءِ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَذَكَرَ حَدِيثَ النُّزُولِ وَأَنَّهُ تَعَالَى يَقُولُ: "مَنْ يَسْتَغْفِرْنِي أَغْفِرْ لَهُ، مَنْ يَسْأَلْنِي أُعْطِهِ ، مَنْ يَدْعُنِي فَأَسْتَجِيبَ لَهُ حَتَّى يَطْلُعَ الْفَجْرُ". فَلِذَلِكَ يَقُولُ: ﴿وَقُرْآنَ الْفَجْرِ إِنَّ قُرْآنَ الْفَجْرِ كَانَ مَشْهُودًا﴾ فَيَشْهَدُهُ اللَّهُ، وَمَلَائِكَةُ اللَّيْلِ، وَمَلَائِكَةُ النَّهَارِ -فَإِنَّهُ تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ زِيَادَةً، وَلَهُ بِهَذَا حَدِيثٌ فِي سُنَنِ أَبِي دَاوُدَ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمِنَ اللَّيْلِ فَتَهَجَّدْ بِهِ نَافِلَةً لَكَ﴾ أَمْرٌ لَهُ بِقِيَامِ اللَّيْلِ بَعْدَ الْمَكْتُوبَةِ، كَمَا وَرَدَ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ سُئِلَ: أَيُّ الصَّلَاةِ أَفْضَلُ بَعْدَ الْمَكْتُوبَةِ؟ قَالَ: "صَلَاةُ اللَّيْلِ" .

وَلِهَذَا أَمَرَ تَعَالَى رَسُولَهُ بَعْدَ الْمَكْتُوبَاتِ بِقِيَامِ اللَّيْلِ، فَإِنَّ التَّهَجُّدَ: مَا كَانَ بَعْدَ نَوْمٍ. قَالَهُ عَلْقَمَةُ، وَالْأَسْوَدُ وَإِبْرَاهِيمُ النَّخَعِيُّ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ وَهُوَ الْمَعْرُوفُ فِي لُغَةِ الْعَرَبِ. وَكَذَلِكَ ثَبَتَتِ الْأَحَادِيثُ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ: أَنَّهُ كَانَ يَتَهَجَّدُ بَعْدَ نَوْمِهِ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَعَائِشَةَ، وَغَيْرِ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ الصَّحَابَةِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ، كَمَا هُوَ مَبْسُوطٌ فِي مَوْضِعِهِ ، وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ وَالْمِنَّةُ.

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ: هُوَ مَا كَانَ بَعْدَ الْعَشَاءِ. وَيُحْمَلُ عَلَى مَا بَعْدَ النَّوْمِ.

وَاخْتُلِفَ فِي مَعْنَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿نَافِلَةً لَكَ﴾ فَقِيلَ: مَعْنَاهُ أَنَّكَ مَخْصُوصٌ بِوُجُوبِ ذَلِكَ وَحْدَكَ، فَجَعَلُوا قِيَامَ اللَّيْلِ وَاجِبًا فِي حَقِّهِ دُونَ الْأُمَّةِ. رَوَاهُ الْعَوْفِيُّ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَهُوَ أَحَدُ قَوْلَيِ الْعُلَمَاءِ، وَأَحَدُ قَوْلَيِ الشَّافِعِيِّ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

وَقِيلَ: إِنَّمَا جُعِلَ قِيَامُ اللَّيْلَ فِي حَقِّهِ نَافِلَةً عَلَى الْخُصُوصِ؛ لِأَنَّهُ قَدْ غُفِرَ لَهُ مَا تَقَدَّمَ مِنْ ذَنْبِهِ وَمَا تَأَخَّرَ، وغيرهُ مِنْ أُمَّتِهِ إِنَّمَا يُكَفِّرُ عَنْهُ صَلَوَاتُهُ النَّوَافِلُ الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي عَلَيْهِ، قَالَهُ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَهُوَ فِي الْمُسْنَدِ عَنْ أَبِي أُمَامَةَ الْبَاهِلِيِّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿عَسَى أَنْ يَبْعَثَكَ رَبُّكَ مَقَامًا مَحْمُودًا﴾ أَيْ: افْعَلْ هَذَا الَّذِي أَمَرْتُكَ بِهِ، لِنُقِيمَكَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ مَقَامًا يَحْسُدُكَ فِيهِ الْخَلَائِقُ كُلُّهُمْ وَخَالِقُهُمْ، تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: قَالَ أَكْثَرُ أَهْلِ التَّأْوِيلِ: ذَلِكَ هُوَ الْمَقَامُ الَّذِي يَقُومُهُ ﷺ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ لِلشَّفَاعَةِ لِلنَّاسِ، لِيُرِيحَهُمْ رَبُّهُمْ مِنْ عَظِيمِ مَا هُمْ فِيهِ مِنْ شِدَّةِ ذَلِكَ الْيَوْمِ.

ذِكْرُ مَنْ قَالَ ذَلِكَ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ بَشَّارٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنْ أَبِي إسحاق، عن صِلَةَ بْنِ زُفَر، عَنْ حُذَيْفَةَ قَالَ: يُجْمَعُ النَّاسُ فِي صَعِيدٍ وَاحِدٍ، يُسْمِعُهُمُ الدَّاعِي وَيَنْفُذُهُمُ الْبَصَرُ، حُفَاةً عُراة كَمَا خُلِقُوا قِيَامًا، لَا تَكَلَّمُ نَفْسٌ إِلَّا بِإِذْنِهِ، يُنَادَى: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، فَيَقُولُ: "لَبَّيْكَ وسعدَيك، وَالْخَيْرُ فِي يَدَيْكَ، وَالشَّرُّ لَيْسَ إِلَيْكَ، وَالْمَهْدِيُّ مَنْ هَدَيْت، وَعَبْدُكَ بَيْنَ يَدَيْكَ، وَبِكَ وَإِلَيْكَ، لَا مَنْجَى وَلَا مَلْجَأَ مِنْكَ إِلَّا إِلَيْكَ، تَبَارَكْتَ وَتَعَالَيْتَ، سُبْحَانَكَ رَبَّ الْبَيْتِ". فَهَذَا الْمَقَامُ الْمَحْمُودُ الَّذِي ذَكَرَهُ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ .

ثُمَّ رَوَاهُ عَنْ بُنْدَار، عَنْ غُنْدَر، عَنْ شُعْبَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، بِهِ . وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ عَنْ مَعْمَرٍ وَالثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، بِهِ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: هَذَا الْمَقَامُ الْمَحْمُودُ مَقَامُ الشَّفَاعَةِ. وَكَذَا قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي نَجِيح، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ. وَقَالَهُ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: هُوَ أَوَّلُ مَنْ تَنْشَقُّ عَنْهُ الْأَرْضُ ، وَأَوَّلُ شَافِعٍ، وَكَانَ أَهْلُ الْعِلْمِ يَرَوْنَ أَنَّهُ الْمَقَامُ الْمَحْمُودُ الَّذِي قَالَ اللَّهُ: ﴿عَسَى أَنْ يَبْعَثَكَ رَبُّكَ مَقَامًا مَحْمُودًا﴾

قُلْتُ: لِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ تَسْلِيمًا تَشْرِيفَاتٌ [يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ] لَا يُشْرِكُهُ فِيهَا أَحَدٌ، وَتَشْرِيفَاتٌ لَا يُسَاوِيهِ فِيهَا أَحَدٌ؛ فَهُوَ أَوَّلُ مَنْ تَنْشَقُّ عَنْهُ الْأَرْضُ وَيُبْعَثُ رَاكِبًا إِلَى الْمَحْشَرِ، وَلَهُ اللِّوَاءُ الَّذِي آدَمُ فَمَنْ دُونَه تَحْتَ لِوَائِهِ، وَلَهُ الْحَوْضُ الَّذِي لَيْسَ فِي الْمَوْقِفِ أَكْثَرُ وَارِدًا مِنْهُ، وَلَهُ الشَّفَاعَةُ الْعُظْمَى عِنْدَ اللَّهِ لِيَأْتِيَ لِفَصْلِ الْقَضَاءِ بَيْنَ الْخَلَائِقِ، وَذَلِكَ بَعْدَمَا يَسْأَلُ النَّاسُ آدَمَ ثُمَّ نُوحًا ثُمَّ إِبْرَاهِيمَ ثُمَّ مُوسَى ثُمَّ عِيسَى، فَكَلٌّ يَقُولُ: "لَسْتُ لَهَا" حَتَّى يَأْتُوا إِلَى مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ فَيَقُولُ: "أَنَا لَهَا، أَنَا لَهَا" كَمَا سَنَذْكُرُ ذَلِكَ مُفَصَّلًا فِي هَذَا الْمَوْضِعِ، إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى. وَمِنْ ذَلِكَ أَنَّهُ يُشَفَّعُ فِي أَقْوَامٍ قَدْ أُمِرَ بِهِمْ إِلَى النَّارِ، فَيُرَدُّونَ عَنْهَا. وَهُوَ أَوَّلُ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ يُقْضَى بَيْنَ أُمَّتِهِ، وَأَوَّلُهُمْ إِجَازَةً عَلَى الصِّرَاطِ بِأُمَّتِهِ. وَهُوَ أَوَّلُ شَفِيعٍ فِي الْجَنَّةِ، كَمَا ثَبَتَ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ. وَفِي حَدِيثِ الصُّورِ: إِنَّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ كُلَّهُمْ لَا يَدْخُلُونَ الْجَنَّةَ إِلَّا بِشَفَاعَتِهِ وَهُوَ أَوَّلُ دَاخِلٍ إِلَيْهَا وَأُمَّتُهُ قَبْلَ الْأُمَمِ كُلِّهِمْ. وَيُشَفَّعُ فِي رَفْعِ دَرَجَاتِ أَقْوَامٍ لَا تَبْلُغُهَا أَعْمَالُهُمْ. وَهُوَ صَاحِبُ الْوَسِيلَةِ الَّتِي هِيَ أَعْلَى مَنْزِلَةٍ فِي الْجَنَّةِ، لَا تَلِيقُ إِلَّا لَهُ. وَإِذَا أَذِنَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى فِي الشَّفَاعَةِ لِلْعُصَاةِ شَفَّعَ الْمَلَائِكَةُ وَالنَّبِيُّونَ وَالْمُؤْمِنُونَ، فَيُشَفَّعُ هُوَ فِي خَلَائِقَ لَا يَعْلَمُ عِدَّتَهُمْ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، وَلَا يُشَفَّعُ أَحَدٌ مِثْلَهُ وَلَا يُسَاوِيهِ فِي ذَلِكَ. وَقَدْ بَسَطْتُ ذَلِكَ مُسْتَقْصًى فِي آخِرِ كِتَابِ "السِّيرَةِ" فِي بَابِ الْخَصَائِصِ، ولله الحمد والمنة.

وَلْنَذْكُرِ الْآنَ الْأَحَادِيثَ الْوَارِدَةَ فِي الْمَقَامِ الْمَحْمُودِ، وَبِاللَّهِ الْمُسْتَعَانُ:

قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ أَبَانٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو الْأَحْوَصِ، عَنْ آدَمَ بْنِ عَلِيٍّ، سَمِعْتُ ابْنَ عُمَرَ [يَقُولُ] : إِنَّ النَّاسَ يَصِيرُونَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ جُثًا، كُلُّ أُمَّةٍ تَتْبَعُ نَبِيَّهَا، يَقُولُونَ: يَا فُلَانُ اشْفَعْ، يَا فُلَانُ اشْفَعْ حَتَّى تَنْتَهِيَ الشَّفَاعَةُ إِلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، فَذَلِكَ يَوْمَ يَبْعَثُهُ اللَّهُ مَقَامًا مَحْمُودًا .

وَرَوَاهُ حَمْزَةُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الْحَكَمِ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعَيْبُ بْنُ اللَّيْثِ، حَدَّثَنِي اللَّيْثُ، عَنْ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أَبِي جَعْفَرٍ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ حَمْزَةَ بْنَ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُمَرَ يَقُولُ: سَمِعْتُ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ عُمَرَ يَقُولُ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ "إِنَّ الشَّمْسَ لَتدنو حَتَّى يَبْلُغَ العَرَقُ نصفَ الْأُذُنِ، فَبَيْنَمَا هُمْ كَذَلِكَ اسْتَغَاثُوا بِآدَمَ، فَيَقُولُ: لَسْتُ صَاحِبَ ذَلِكَ، ثُمَّ بِمُوسَى فَيَقُولُ كَذَلِكَ، ثُمَّ بِمُحَمَّدٍ فَيَشْفَعُ بَيْنَ الْخَلْقِ ، فَيَمْشِي حَتَّى يَأْخُذَ بِحَلْقَةِ بَابِ الْجَنَّةِ، فَيَوْمَئِذٍ يَبْعَثُهُ اللَّهُ مَقَامًا مَحْمُودًا". [يَحْمَدُهُ أَهْلُ الْجَنَّةِ كُلُّهُمْ] .

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ فِي "الزَّكَاةِ" عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ بُكَيْر، وَعَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ صَالِحٍ، كِلَاهُمَا عَنِ اللَّيْثِ بْنِ سَعْدٍ، بِهِ ، وَزَادَ "فَيَوْمَئِذٍ يَبْعَثُهُ اللَّهُ مَقَامًا محمودًا، بحمده أَهْلُ الْجَمْعِ كُلُّهُمْ".

قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: وَحَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ عَيَّاش، حَدَّثَنَا شُعَيْبُ بْنُ أَبِي حَمْزة، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ المُنْكَدِر، عَنْ جَابِرِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "مَنْ قَالَ حِينَ يَسْمَعُ النِّدَاءَ: اللَّهُمَّ رَبَّ هَذِهِ الدَّعْوَةِ التَّامَّةِ، وَالصَّلَاةِ الْقَائِمَةِ، آتِ مُحَمَّدًا الْوَسِيلَةَ وَالْفَضِيلَةَ، وَابْعَثْهُ مَقَامًا مَحْمُودًا الَّذِي وَعَدْتَهُ، حَلَّت لَهُ شَفَاعَتِي يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ". انْفَرَدَ بِهِ دُونَ مُسْلِمٍ .

حَدِيثُ أُبَيٍّ:

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَامِرٍ الْأَزْدِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا زُهَيْرِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَقِيلٍ، عَنِ الطُّفَيْلِ بْنِ أُبَيِّ بْنِ كَعْبٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِذَا كَانَ يَوْمُ الْقِيَامَةِ، كَنْتُ إِمَامَ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ وَخَطِيبَهُمْ، وَصَاحِبَ شَفَاعَتِهِمْ غَيْرَ فَخْر" .

وَأَخْرَجَهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي عَامِرٍ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ بْنِ عَمْرو العَقَديّ، وَقَالَ: "حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ ". وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَقِيلٍ بِهِ. وَقَدْ قَدَّمْنَا فِي حَدِيثِ: "أُبَيِّ بْنِ كَعْبٍ" فِي قِرَاءَةِ الْقُرْآنِ عَلَى سَبْعَةِ أَحْرُفٍ، قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ في آخِرِهِ: "فَقُلْتُ: اللَّهُمَّ، اغْفِرْ لِأُمَّتِي، اللَّهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِأُمَّتِي، وَأَخَّرْتُ الثَّالِثَةَ لِيَوْمٍ يَرْغَبُ إِلَيَّ فِيهِ الْخَلْقُ، حَتَّى إبراهيم عليه السلام" .

حَدِيثُ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ:

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ سَعِيدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدُ بْنُ أَبِي عَرُوبة، حَدَّثَنَا قَتَادَةَ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "يَجْتَمِعُ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، فَيُلْهَمُونَ ذَلِكَ فَيَقُولُونَ: لَوِ اسْتَشْفَعْنَا إِلَى رَبِّنَا، فَأَرَاحَنَا مِنْ مَكَانِنَا هَذَا. فَيَأْتُونَ آدَمَ فَيَقُولُونَ: يَا آدَمُ، أَنْتَ أَبُو الْبَشَرِ، خَلَقَكَ اللَّهُ بِيَدِهِ، وَأَسْجَدَ لَكَ مَلَائِكَتَهُ، وَعَلَّمَكَ أَسْمَاءَ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ، فَاشْفَعْ لَنَا إِلَى رَبِّكَ حَتَّى يُرِيحَنَا مِنْ مَكَانِنَا هَذَا. فَيَقُولُ لَهُمْ آدَمُ: لَسْتُ هُنَاكُمْ، وَيَذْكُرُ ذَنْبَهُ الَّذِي أَصَابَ، فَيَسْتَحْيِي رَبَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، مِنْ ذَلِكَ، وَيَقُولُ: وَلَكِنِ ائْتُوا نُوحًا، فَإِنَّهُ أَوَّلُ رَسُولٍ بَعَثَهُ اللَّهُ إِلَى أَهْلِ الْأَرْضِ. فَيَأْتُونَ نُوحًا فَيَقُولُ: لَسْتُ هُنَاكُمْ، وَيَذْكُرُ خَطِيئَةَ سُؤَالَهُ رَبَّهُ مَا لَيْسَ لَهُ بِهِ عِلْمٌ، فَيَسْتَحْيِي رَبَّهُ مِنْ ذَلِكَ، وَلَكِنِ ائْتُوا إِبْرَاهِيمَ خَلِيلَ الرَّحْمَنِ. فَيَأْتُونَهُ فَيَقُولُ: لَسْتُ هُنَاكُمْ، وَلَكِنِ ائْتُوا مُوسَى، عَبْدًا كَلَّمَهُ اللَّهُ، وَأَعْطَاهُ التَّوْرَاةَ. فَيَأْتُونَ مُوسَى فَيَقُولُ: لَسْتُ هُنَاكُمْ، وَيَذْكُرُ لَهُمُ النَّفْسَ الَّتِي قَتَلَ بِغَيْرِ نَفْسٍ فَيَسْتَحْيِي رَبَّهُ مِنْ ذَلِكَ، وَلَكِنِ ائْتُوا عِيسَى عَبْدَ اللَّهِ وَرَسُولَهُ، وَكَلِمَتَهُ وَرُوحَهُ، فَيَأْتُونَ عِيسَى فَيَقُولُ: لَسْتُ هُنَاكُمْ، وَلَكِنِ ائْتُوا مُحَمَّدًا عَبْدًا غُفِرَ لَهُ مَا تَقَدَّمَ مِنْ ذَنْبِهِ وَمَا تَأَخَّرَ فَيَأْتُونِي". قَالَ الْحَسَنُ هَذَا الْحَرْفُ : "فَأَقُومُ فَأَمْشِي بَيْنَ سِماطين مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ". قَالَ أَنَسٌ: "حَتَّى أَسْتَأْذِنَ عَلَى رَبِّي، فَإِذَا رَأَيْتُ رَبِّي وَقَعْتُ لَهُ -أَوْ: خَرَرْتُ -سَاجِدًا لِرَبِّي، فَيَدَعُنِي مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ أَنْ يَدَعَنِي". قَالَ: "ثُمَّ يُقَالُ: ارْفَعْ مُحَمَّدُ، قُلْ يُسْمَعْ، وَاشْفَعْ تَشَفَّعْ، وَسَلْ تُعْطَهُ. فَأَرْفَعُ رَأْسِي، فَأَحْمَدُهُ بِتَحْمِيدٍ يُعَلِّمُنيه، ثُمَّ أَشْفَعُ فَيَحُدُّ لِي حَدًّا، فَأُدْخِلُهُمُ الْجَنَّةَ": "ثُمَّ أَعُودُ إِلَيْهِ الثَّانِيَةَ، فَإِذَا رَأَيْتُ رَبِّي وَقَعْتُ -أَوْ: خَرَرْتُ -سَاجِدًا لِرَبِّي، فَيَدَعُنِي مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ أَنْ يَدَعَنِي. ثُمَّ يُقَالُ: ارْفَعْ مُحَمَّدُ، قُلْ يُسْمَعْ، وَسَلْ تُعْطَهُ، وَاشْفَعْ تُشَفَّعْ. فَأَرْفَعُ رَأْسِي فَأَحْمَدُهُ بِتَحْمِيدٍ يُعَلِّمُنيه، ثُمَّ أَشْفَعُ فَيَحُدُّ لِي حَدًّا، فَأُدْخِلُهُمُ الْجَنَّةَ، ثُمَّ أَعُودُ فِي الثَّالِثَةِ؛ فَإِذَا رَأَيْتُ رَبِّي وَقَعْتُ -أَوْ: خَرَرْتُ -سَاجِدًا لِرَبِّي، فَيَدَعُنِي مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ أَنْ يَدَعَنِي، ثُمَّ يُقَالُ: ارْفَعْ مُحَمَّدُ، قُلْ يُسْمَعْ، وَسَلْ تُعْطَهُ، وَاشْفَعْ تُشَفَّعْ. فَأَرْفَعُ رَأْسِي فَأَحْمَدُهُ بِتَحْمِيدٍ يُعَلِّمُنيه ثُمَّ أَشْفَعُ فَيَحُدُّ لِي حَدًّا فَأُدْخِلُهُمُ الْجَنَّةَ. ثُمَّ أَعُودُ الرَّابِعَةَ فَأَقُولُ: يَا رَبِّ، مَا بَقِيَ إِلَّا مَنْ حَبَسَهُ الْقُرْآنُ". فَحَدَّثَنَا أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ أَنَّ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ قَالَ: "فَيَخْرُجُ مِنَ النَّارِ مَنْ قَالَ: "لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ" وَكَانَ فِي قَلْبِهِ مِنَ الْخَيْرِ مَا يَزِنُ شَعِيْرَةً، ثُمَّ يَخْرُجُ مِنَ النَّارِ مَنْ قَالَ: "لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ" وَكَانَ فِي قَلْبِهِ مِنَ الْخَيْرِ مَا يَزِنُ بُرَّة ثُمَّ يَخْرُجُ مِنَ النَّارِ مَنْ قَالَ: "لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ" وَكَانَ فِي قَلْبِهِ مِنَ الْخَيْرِ مَا يَزِنُ ذَرَّةً".

أَخْرَجَاهُ [فِي الصَّحِيحِ] مِنْ حَدِيثِ سَعِيدٍ، بِهِ وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ، عَنْ عَفَّانَ، عَنْ حَمَّادِ بْنِ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ ثَابِتٍ، عَنْ أنس بطوله .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا حَرْبُ بْنُ مَيْمُونٍ أَبُو الْخَطَّابِ الْأَنْصَارِيُّ، عَنِ النَّضْرِ بْنِ أَنَسٍ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ قَالَ: حَدَّثَنِي نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنِّي لَقَائِمٌ أَنْتَظِرُ أُمَّتِي تَعْبُرُ الصِّرَاطَ، إِذْ جَاءَنِي عِيسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فَقَالَ: هَذِهِ الْأَنْبِيَاءُ قَدْ جَاءَتْكَ يَا مُحَمَّدُ يَسْأَلُونَ -أَوْ قَالَ: يَجْتَمِعُونَ إِلَيْكَ -ويَدْعُون اللَّهَ أَنْ يُفَرِّقَ بَيْنَ جَمِيعِ الْأُمَمِ إِلَى حَيْثُ يَشَاءُ اللَّهُ، لِغَمِّ مَا هُمْ فِيهِ، فَالْخَلْقُ مُلجَمون بِالْعَرَقِ، فَأَمَّا الْمُؤْمِنُ فَهُوَ عَلَيْهِ كالزكْمَة، وَأَمَّا الْكَافِرُ فَيَغْشَاهُ الْمَوْتُ، فَقَالَ: انْتَظِرْ حَتَّى أَرْجِعَ إِلَيْكَ. فَذَهَبَ نَبِيُّ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَقَامَ تَحْتَ الْعَرْشِ، فَلَقِيَ مَا لَمْ يَلْقَ مَلَك مُصْطَفًى وَلَا نَبِيٌّ مُرْسَلٌ. فَأَوْحَى اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، إِلَى جِبْرِيلَ: أَنِ اذْهَبْ إِلَى مُحَمَّدٍ، وَقُلْ لَهُ: ارْفَعْ رَأْسَكَ، وَسَلْ تُعطَه، وَاشْفَعْ تُشَفَّعْ. فشفَعتُ فِي أُمَّتِي: أَنْ أُخْرِجَ مِنْ كُلِّ تِسْعَةٍ وَتِسْعِينَ إِنْسَانًا وَاحِدًا. فَمَا زِلْتُ أَتَرَدَّدُ إِلَى رَبِّي، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، فَلَا أَقْوَمُ مِنْهُ مَقَامًا إِلَّا شُفِّعْتُ، حَتَّى أَعْطَانِي اللَّهُ مِنْ ذَلِكَ، أَنْ قَالَ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، أَدْخِلْ [مِنْ أُمَّتِكَ] مِنْ خَلْقِ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، مَنْ شَهِدَ أَنْ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ يَوْمًا وَاحِدًا مُخْلِصًا وَمَاتَ عَلَى ذَلِكَ " .

حَدِيثُ بُرَيْدَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ:

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ بْنُ حَنْبَلٍ: حَدَّثَنَا الْأَسْوَدُ بْنُ عَامِرٍ، أَخْبَرَنَا أَبُو إِسْرَائِيلَ، عَنِ الْحَارِثِ بْنِ حَصِيرة، عَنِ ابْنِ بُرَيْدة، عَنْ أَبِيهِ: أَنَّهُ دَخَلَ عَلَى مُعَاوِيَةَ، فَإِذَا رَجُلٌ يَتَكَلَّمُ، فَقَالَ بُرَيْدَةُ: يَا مُعَاوِيَةُ، تَأْذَنُ لِي فِي الْكَلَامِ؟ فَقَالَ: نَعَمْ -وَهُوَ يَرَى أَنَّهُ يَتَكَلَّمُ بِمِثْلِ مَا قَالَ الْآخَرُ -فَقَالَ بُرَيْدَةُ: سمعتُ رسولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "إِنِّي لَأَرْجُوَ أَنْ أُشَفَّعَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ عَدَدَ مَا عَلَى الْأَرْضِ مِنْ شَجَرَةٍ وَمَدَرَةٍ". قَالَ: فَتَرْجُوهَا أَنْتَ يَا مُعَاوِيَةُ، وَلَا يَرْجُوهَا عَلِيٌّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ؟! .

حَدِيثُ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ:

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَارِمُ بْنُ الْفَضْلِ، حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدُ بْنُ زَيْدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحَكَمِ البُنَاني، عَنْ عُثْمَانَ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَنْ عَلْقَمَةَ وَالْأَسْوَدِ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ قَالَ: جَاءَ ابْنَا مُلَيْكَة إِلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ فَقَالَا إِنَّ أمَّنا [كَانَتْ] تُكْرِمُ الزَّوْجَ، وَتَعْطِفُ عَلَى الْوَلَدِ -قَالَ: وَذَكَرَ الضَّيْفَ -غَيْرَ أَنَّهَا كَانَتْ وَأَدَتْ فِي الْجَاهِلِيَّةِ؟ فَقَالَ: "أُمُّكُمَا فِي النَّارِ". قَالَ: فَأَدْبَرَا وَالسُّوءُ يُرَى فِي وُجُوهِهِمَا، فَأُمِرَ بِهِمَا فَرُدَّا، فَرَجَعَا وَالسُّرُورُ يُرَى فِي وُجُوهِهِمَا؛ رَجَاءَ أَنْ يَكُونَ قَدْ حَدَثَ شَيْءٌ، فَقَالَ: "أُمِّي مَعَ أُمِّكُمَا". فَقَالَ رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ: وَمَا يُغْنِي هَذَا عَنْ أُمِّهِ شَيْئًا! وَنَحْنُ نَطَأُ عَقِبَيْهِ. فَقَالَ رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ -وَلَمْ أَرَ رَجُلًا قَطُّ أَكْثَرَ سُؤَالًا مِنْهُ-: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، هَلْ وَعَدَكَ رَبُّكَ فِيهَا أَوْ فِيهِمَا؟. قَالَ: فَظَنَّ أَنَّهُ مِنْ شَيْءٍ قَدْ سَمِعَهُ، فَقَالَ: "مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ رَبِّي وَمَا أَطْمَعَنِي فِيهِ، وَإِنِّي لَأَقُومُ الْمَقَامَ الْمَحْمُودَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ". فقالَ الْأَنْصَارِيُّ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، وَمَا ذَاكَ المقام المحمود؟ قال:" ذاك إذا جِيءَ بِكُمْ حُفَاةً عُرَاةً غُرْلًا فَيَكُونُ أَوَّلَ مَنْ يُكْسَى إِبْرَاهِيمُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فَيَقُولُ: اكْسُوا خَلِيلِي. فَيُؤْتَى بِرَيْطَتَيْنِ بَيْضَاوَيْنِ، فَيَلْبَسُهُمَا ثُمَّ يُقْعِدُهُ مُسْتَقْبِلَ الْعَرْشِ، ثُمَّ أُوتَى بِكِسْوَتِي فَأَلْبَسُهَا، فَأَقُومُ عَنْ يَمِينِهِ مَقَامًا لَا يَقُومُهُ أَحَدٌ، فَيَغْبِطُنِي فِيهِ الْأَوَّلُونَ وَالْآخِرُونَ. وَيُفْتَحُ نَهْرٌ مِنَ الْكَوْثَرِ إِلَى الْحَوْضِ". فَقَالَ الْمُنَافِقُونَ: إِنَّهُ مَا جَرَى مَاءٌ قَطُّ إِلَّا عَلَى حَالٍ أَوْ رَضْرَاضٍ. فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ "حَالُهُ الْمِسْكُ، وَرَضْرَاضُهُ التُّوم". [قَالَ الْمُنَافِقُ: لَمْ أَسْمَعْ كَالْيَوْمِ. قلَّما جَرَى مَاءٌ قَطُّ عَلَى حَالٍ أَوْ رَضْرَاضٍ، إِلَّا كَانَ لَهُ نَبْتَةٌ. فَقَالَ الْأَنْصَارِيُّ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، هَلْ لَهُ نَبْتٌ؟ قَالَ "نَعَمْ، قُضْبَانُ الذَّهَبِ"] . قَالَ الْمُنَافِقُ: لَمْ أَسْمَعْ كَالْيَوْمِ، فَإِنَّهُ قَلَّمَا يَنْبُتُ قَضِيبٌ إِلَّا أَوْرَقَ، وَإِلَّا كَانَ لَهُ ثَمَرٌ! قَالَ الْأَنْصَارِيُّ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، هَلْ لَهُ ثَمَرَةٌ؟ قَالَ: "نَعَمْ، أَلْوَانُ الْجَوْهَرِ، وَمَاؤُهُ أَشَدَّ بَيَاضًا مِنَ اللَّبَنِ، وَأَحْلَى مِنَ الْعَسَلِ، مَنْ شَرِبَ مِنْهُ شَرْبَةً لَا يَظْمَأُ بَعْدَهُ، وَمَنْ حُرِمَهُ لَمْ يَرْوَ بَعْدَهُ" .

وَقَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ الطَّيَالِسِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ سَلَمَة بْنِ كُهَيْل، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ أَبِي الزّعْرَاء، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: ثُمَّ يَأْذَنُ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، فِي الشَّفَاعَةِ، فَيَقُومُ رُوحُ الْقُدُسِ جِبْرِيلُ، ثُمَّ يَقُومُ إِبْرَاهِيمُ خَلِيلُ اللَّهِ، ثُمَّ يَقُومُ عِيسَى أَوْ مُوسَى -قَالَ أَبُو الزَّعْرَاءِ: لَا أَدْرِي أَيَّهُمَا -قَالَ: ثُمَّ يَقُومُ نَبِيُّكُمْ ﷺ رَابِعًا، فَيَشْفَعُ لَا يَشْفَعُ أَحَدٌ بَعْدَهُ أَكْثَرَ مِمَّا شَفَعَ، وَهُوَ الْمَقَامُ الْمَحْمُودُ الَّذِي قَالَ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿عَسَى أَنْ يَبْعَثَكَ رَبُّكَ مَقَامًا مَحْمُودًا﴾ .

حَدِيثُ كَعْبِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ:

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ رَبِّهِ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ حَرْبٍ، حَدَّثَنَا الزُّبَيْدِيُّ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ [بْنِ كَعْبِ] بْنِ مَالِكٍ، عَنْ كَعْبِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "يُبْعَثُ النَّاسُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، فَأَكُونُ أَنَا وَأُمَّتِي عَلَى تَلٍّ، وَيَكْسُونِي رَبِّي، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، حُلَّةً خَضْرَاءَ ثُمَّ يُؤْذَنُ لِي فَأَقُولُ مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ أَنْ أَقُولَ، فَذَلِكَ الْمَقَامُ الْمَحْمُودُ" .

حَدِيثُ أَبِي الدَّرْدَاءِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ:

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا حَسَنٌ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ لَهِيعة، حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ أَبِي حَبِيبٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ ابن جُبَير، عَنْ أَبِي الدَّرْدَاءِ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَنَا أَوَّلُ مَنْ يُؤْذَنُ لَهُ بِالسُّجُودِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، وَأَنَا أَوَّلُ مَنْ يُؤْذَنُ لَهُ أَنْ يَرْفَعَ رَأْسَهُ، فَأَنْظُرُ إِلَى مَا بَيْنَ يَدِي، فَأَعْرِفُ أُمَّتِي مِنْ بَيْنِ الْأُمَمِ، وَمِنْ خَلْفِي مِثْلَ ذَلِكَ، وَعَنْ يَمِينِي مِثْلَ ذَلِكَ، وَعَنْ شِمَالِي مِثْلَ ذَلِكَ". فَقَالَ رَجُلٌ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، كَيْفَ تَعْرِفُ أُمَّتَكَ مِنْ بَيْنِ الْأُمَمِ، فِيمَا بَيْنَ نُوحٍ إِلَى أُمَّتِكَ؟ قَالَ: "هُمْ غُرٌّ مُحَجَّلُون، مِنْ أَثَرِ الْوُضُوءِ، لَيْسَ أَحَدٌ كَذَلِكَ غَيْرُهُمْ، وَأَعْرِفُهُمْ أَنَّهُمْ يُؤتَونَ كُتُبَهُمْ بِأَيْمَانِهِمْ، وَأَعْرِفُهُمْ تَسْعَى بين أيديهم ذريتهم" .

حَدِيثُ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ:

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ سَعِيدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو حَيَّان، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو زُرْعَة بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ جَرِيرٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، قَالَ: أَتَى رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِلَحْمٍ، فَرُفع إِلَيْهِ الذِّرَاعُ -وَكَانَتْ تَعْجِبُهُ -فَنَهَسَ مِنْهَا نَهْسة ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: "أَنَا سَيِّدُ النَّاسِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، وَهَلْ تَدْرُونَ مِمَّ ذَاكَ؟ يَجْمَعُ اللَّهُ الْأَوَّلِينَ وَالْآخَرِينَ فِي صَعِيدٍ وَاحِدٍ، يُسْمعهم الدَّاعِي ويَنفذُهم الْبَصَرُ، وَتَدْنُو الشَّمْسُ فَيَبْلُغُ النَّاسَ مِنَ الْغَمِّ وَالْكَرْبِ مَا لَا يُطِيقُونَ وَلَا يَحْتَمِلُونَ. فَيَقُولُ بَعْضُ النَّاسِ لِبَعْضٍ: [أَلَّا تَرَوْنَ إِلَى مَا أَنْتُمْ فِيهِ؟ أَلَا تَرَوْنَ إِلَى مَا قَدْ بَلَغَكُمْ؟ أَلَا تَنْظُرُونَ مَنْ يَشْفَعُ لَكُمْ إِلَى رَبِّكُمْ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ؟ فَيَقُولُ بَعْضُ النَّاسِ لِبَعْضٍ] : أَبُوكُمْ آدَمُ!.

فَيَأْتُونَ آدَمَ، فَيَقُولُونَ: يَا آدَمُ، أَنْتَ أَبُو الْبَشَرِ، خَلَقَكَ اللَّهُ بِيَدِهِ، وَنَفَخَ فِيكَ مِنْ رُوحِهِ، وَأَمَرَ الْمَلَائِكَةَ فَسَجَدُوا لَكَ؛ فَاشْفَعْ لَنَا إِلَى رَبِّكَ، أَلَا تَرَى مَا نَحْنُ فِيهِ؟ أَلَا تَرَى مَا قَدْ بَلَغَنَا؟ فَيَقُولُ آدَمُ: إِنَّ رَبِّي قَدْ غَضِبَ الْيَوْمَ غَضَبًا لَمْ يَغْضَبْ قَبْلَهُ مِثْلَهُ، وَلَنْ يَغْضَبْ بَعْدَهُ مِثْلَهُ، وَإِنَّهُ نَهَانِي عَنِ الشَّجَرَةِ فَعَصَيْتُهُ، نَفْسِي، نَفْسِي، نَفْسِي! اذْهَبُوا إِلَى غَيْرِي، اذْهَبُوا إِلَى نُوحٍ.

فَيَأْتُونَ نُوحًا فَيَقُولُونَ: يَا نُوحُ، أَنْتَ أَوَّلُ الرُّسُلِ إِلَى أَهْلِ الْأَرْضِ، وَسَمَّاكَ اللَّهُ عَبْدًا شَكُورًا، اشْفَعْ لَنَا إِلَى رَبِّكَ، أَلَا تَرَى مَا نَحْنُ فِيهِ؟ أَلَا تَرَى مَا قَدْ بَلَغَنَا؟ فَيَقُولُ نُوحٌ: إِنَّ رَبِّي قَدْ غَضِبَ الْيَوْمَ غَضَبًا لَمْ يَغْضَبْ قَبْلَهُ مِثْلَهُ، وَلَنْ يَغْضَبْ بَعْدَهُ مِثْلَهُ، وَإِنَّهُ كَانَتْ لِي دَعْوَةٌ عَلَى قَوْمِي، نَفْسِي، نَفْسِي، نَفْسِي! اذْهَبُوا إِلَى غَيْرِي، اذْهَبُوا إِلَى إِبْرَاهِيمَ.

فَيَأْتُونَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ فَيَقُولُونَ: يَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ، أَنْتَ نَبِيُّ اللَّهِ وَخَلِيلُهُ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْأَرْضِ، [اشْفَعْ لَنَا إِلَى رَبِّكَ] أَلَا تَرَى مَا نَحْنُ فِيهِ؟ أَلَا تَرَى مَا قَدْ بَلَغَنَا؟ فَيَقُولُ: إِنَّ رَبِّي قَدْ غَضِبَ الْيَوْمَ غَضَبًا لَمْ يَغْضَبْ قَبْلَهُ مِثْلَهُ، وَلَنْ يَغْضَبْ بَعْدَهُ مِثْلَهُ، فَذَكَرَ كَذِبَاتِهِ نَفْسِي، نَفْسِي، نَفْسِي [اذْهَبُوا إِلَى غَيْرِي] اذْهَبُوا إِلَى مُوسَى.

فَيَأْتُونَ مُوسَى فَيَقُولُونَ: يَا مُوسَى، أَنْتَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ، اصْطَفَاكَ اللَّهُ بِرِسَالَاتِهِ وَبِكَلَامِهِ عَلَى النَّاسِ، اشْفَعْ لَنَا إِلَى رَبِّكَ، أَلَا تَرَى مَا نَحْنُ فِيهِ؟ أَلَا تَرَى مَا قَدْ بَلَغَنَا؟ فَيَقُولُ لَهُمْ مُوسَى: إِنَّ رَبِّي قَدْ غَضِبَ الْيَوْمَ غَضَبًا لَمْ يَغْضَبْ قَبْلَهُ مِثْلَهُ، وَلَنْ يَغْضَبْ بَعْدَهُ مِثْلَهُ، وَإِنِّي قَتَلْتُ نَفْسًا لَمْ أُومَرْ بِقَتْلِهَا، نَفْسِي، نَفْسِي، نَفْسِي، اذْهَبُوا إِلَى غَيْرِي، اذْهَبُوا إِلَى عِيسَى.

فَيَأْتُونَ عِيسَى فَيَقُولُونَ: يَا عِيسَى، أَنْتَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ وَكَلِمَتُهُ أَلْقَاهَا إِلَى مَرْيَمَ وَرُوحٌ مِنْهُ -قَالَ: هَكَذَا هُوَ -وَكَلَّمْتَ النَّاسَ فِي الْمَهْدِ، فَاشْفَعْ لَنَا إِلَى رَبِّكَ، أَلَا تَرَى مَا نَحْنُ فِيهِ؟ أَلَا تَرَى مَا قَدْ بَلَغَنَا؟ فَيَقُولُ لَهُمْ عِيسَى: إِنَّ رَبِّي قَدْ غَضِبَ الْيَوْمَ غَضَبًا لَمْ يَغْضَبْ قَبْلَهُ مِثْلَهُ، وَلَنْ يَغْضَبْ بَعْدَهُ مِثْلَهُ، وَلَمْ يَذْكُرْ ذَنْبًا، اذْهَبُوا إِلَى غَيْرِي، اذْهَبُوا إِلَى مُحَمَّدٍ.
