## 17:97 — verse 97

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing of His disposal over His creation, the executing of His judgment, and that there is none who can overturn it, that whoever He guides, none can lead astray, {and whoever He sends astray, you will never find for them protectors besides Him}, meaning: guiding them, as He said: {Whoever Allah guides is the rightly guided, and whoever He sends astray, you will never find for him a guiding protector} [al-Kahf: 17].

Regarding His statement, {And We will gather them on the Day of Resurrection upon their faces}, Imam Ahmad said:

[chain] I heard Anas ibn Malik say: It was said, "O Messenger of Allah, how will people be gathered upon their faces?" He said: "The One who made them walk upon their feet is able to make them walk upon their faces." Both al-Bukhari and Muslim reported it in their Sahihs.

Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] from Hudhayfah ibn Asid, who said: Abu Dharr stood up and said: "O Banu Ghifar, speak but do not swear oaths, for the truthful one, believed as truthful, told me that people will be gathered in three groups: a group riding, fed and clothed; a group walking and hastening on foot; and a group whom the angels drag upon their faces and gather to the Fire." One of those present said: "We understand these two, but what about those who walk and hasten?" He said: "Allah, Mighty and Majestic, will cast affliction upon the backs (of riding animals) until no mount remains, so much so that a man who has a delightful garden would offer it in exchange for an old worn-out she-camel fit for a saddle, and still not be able to obtain it."

Regarding His statement, {blind}, meaning: they will not see, {and dumb}, meaning: they will not speak, {and deaf}: they will not hear. This will occur in one state but not another, as a recompense for them, just as they were in this world dumb, blind, and deaf to the truth, so they are recompensed in their place of gathering with this at the very time they most need it. {Their abode}, meaning: their place of return and their final destination, {is Hell; every time it subsides} Ibn Abbas said: it quiets down. Mujahid said: it dies down. {We increase for them its blaze}, meaning: flame, intense heat, and glowing embers, as He said: {So taste it, for We will not increase you except in torment} [al-Naba: 30].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ تَصَرُّفِهِ فِي خَلْقِهِ، وَنُفُوذِ حُكْمِهِ، وَأَنَّهُ لَا مُعَقِّبَ لَهُ، بِأَنَّهُ مَنْ يَهْدِهِ فَلَا مُضِلَّ لَهُ (وَمَنْ يُضْلِلْ فَلَنْ تَجِدَ لَهُمْ أَوْلِيَاءَ مِنْ دُونِهِ) أَيْ: يَهْدُونَهُمْ، كما قَالَ: ﴿مَنْ يَهْدِ اللَّهُ فَهُوَ الْمُهْتَدِي وَمَنْ يُضْلِلْ فَلَنْ تَجِدَ لَهُ وَلِيًّا مُرْشِدًا﴾ [الْكَهْفِ: ١٧] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: (وَنَحْشُرُهُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ عَلَى وُجُوهِهِمْ) قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ نُمَيْرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ عَنْ نُفَيْع قَالَ : سَمِعْتُ أَنَسَ بْنَ مَالِكٍ يَقُولُ: قِيلَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، كَيْفَ يُحْشَرُ النَّاسُ عَلَى وُجُوهِهِمْ؟ قَالَ: "الَّذِي أَمْشَاهُمْ عَلَى أَرْجُلِهِمْ قَادِرٌ عَلَى أَنْ يُمْشِيَهُمْ عَلَى وُجُوهِهِمْ". وَأَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا: [حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ] ، حَدَّثَنَا الْوَلِيدُ بْنُ جُمَيْع الْقُرَشِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو الطُّفَيْلِ عَامِرِ بْنِ وَاثِلَةَ، عَنْ حُذَيْفَةَ بْنِ أُسَيْدٍ قَالَ: قَامَ أَبُو ذَرٍّ فَقَالَ: يَا بَنِي غِفَارٍ، قُولُوا وَلَا تَحْلِفُوا، فَإِنَّ الصَّادِقَ الْمَصْدُوقَ حَدَّثَنِي: أَنَّ النَّاسَ يُحْشَرُونَ عَلَى ثَلَاثَةِ أَفْوَاجٍ: فَوْجٍ رَاكِبِينَ طَاعِمِينَ كَاسِينَ، وَفَوْجٍ يَمْشُونَ وَيَسْعَوْنَ، وَفَوْجٍ تَسْحَبُهُمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ عَلَى وُجُوهِهِمْ وَتَحْشُرُهُمْ إِلَى النَّارِ. فَقَالَ قَائِلٌ مِنْهُمْ: هَذَانِ قَدْ عَرَفْنَاهُمَا، فَمَا بَالُ الَّذِينَ يَمْشُونَ وَيَسْعَوْنَ ؟ قَالَ: يُلْقِي اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، الْآفَةَ عَلَى الظَّهْرِ حَتَّى لَا يَبْقَى ظَهْرٌ، حَتَّى إِنَّ الرَّجُلَ لَتَكُونُ لَهُ الْحَدِيقَةُ الْمُعْجِبَةُ، فَيُعْطِيهَا بِالشَّارِفِ ذَاتِ الْقَتَبِ، فَلَا يَقْدِرُ عليها .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: (عُمْيًا) أَيْ: لَا يُبْصِرُونَ (وَبُكْمًا) يَعْنِي: لَا يَنْطِقُونَ (وَصُمًّا) : لَا يَسْمَعُونَ. وَهَذَا يَكُونُ فِي حَالٍ دُونَ حَالٍ جَزَاءً لَهُمْ كَمَا كَانُوا فِي الدُّنْيَا بُكْمًا وَعُمْيًا وَصُمًّا عَنِ الْحَقِّ فَجُوزُوا فِي مَحْشَرِهِمْ بِذَلِكَ أَحْوَجَ مَا يَحْتَاجُونَ إِلَيْهِ (مَأْوَاهُمْ) أَيْ: مُنْقَلِبُهُمْ وَمَصِيرُهُمْ (جَهَنَّمُ كُلَّمَا خَبَتْ) قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: سَكَنَتْ . وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: طَفِئَتْ (زِدْنَاهُمْ سَعِيرًا) أَيْ: لَهَبًا وَوَهَجًا وَجَمْرًا، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿فَذُوقُوا فَلَنْ نَزِيدَكُمْ إِلا عَذَابًا﴾ [النَّبَإِ: ٣٠] .

---

## 17:98-99 — verses 98-99 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: this, that with which We have recompensed them, namely being resurrected in blindness, dumbness, and deafness, is the recompense they deserve, because they denied {Our signs}, meaning Our proofs and evidences, and considered the occurrence of resurrection improbable, {and they said, "When we are bones and crumbled particles,"} decayed and disintegrated, {"shall we truly be resurrected as a new creation?"} meaning: after we have become what we have become, of decay and destruction, of dispersal and disappearance into the earth, shall we be brought back a second time? So the Almighty presented an argument against them and alerted them to His power over that, in that He created the heavens and the earth, and so His power to bring them back is easier than that, as He said: {The creation of the heavens and the earth is greater than the creation of mankind} [Ghafir: 57]. And He said: {Have they not seen that Allah, who created the heavens and the earth and did not tire from creating them, is able to give life to the dead? Yes indeed, He has power over all things} [al-Ahqaf: 33]. And He said: {Is not He who created the heavens and the earth able to create the like of them? Yes indeed, and He is the All-Knowing Creator. His command, when He wills a thing, is only to say to it, "Be," and it is. So glory be to Him in whose hand is the dominion of all things, and to Him you will be returned} [Ya-Sin: 81-83].

And here He says: {Have they not seen that Allah, who created the heavens and the earth, is able to create the like of them?} meaning: on the Day of Resurrection He will bring back their bodies and originate them in another formation, and restore them just as He began them.

His saying, {and He has set for them a term about which there is no doubt}, means: He has set for their return and their being raised up from their graves a fixed term and a determined period which must inevitably run its course, as the Almighty said: {and We do not delay it except for a term already determined} [Hud: 104].

His saying, {yet the wrongdoers refuse}, meaning: after the argument has been established against them, {except disbelief}, meaning nothing but persistence in their falsehood and misguidance.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: هَذَا الَّذِي جَازَيْنَاهُمْ بِهِ، مِنَ الْبَعْثِ عَلَى الْعَمَى وَالْبُكْمِ وَالصَّمَمِ، جَزَاؤُهُمُ الَّذِي يَسْتَحِقُّونَهُ؛ لِأَنَّهُمْ كَذَّبُوا (بِآيَاتِنَا) أَيْ بِأَدِلَّتِنَا وَحُجَجِنَا، وَاسْتَبْعَدُوا وُقُوعَ الْبَعْثِ (وَقَالُوا أَئِذَا كُنَّا عِظَامًا وَرُفَاتًا) بَالِيَةً نَخِرَةً (أَئِنَّا لَمَبْعُوثُونَ خَلْقًا جَدِيدًا) أَيْ: بَعْدَ مَا صِرْنَا إِلَى مَا صِرْنَا إِلَيْهِ مِنَ الْبِلَى وَالْهَلَاكِ، وَالتَّفَرُّقِ وَالذَّهَابِ فِي الْأَرْضِ نُعَادُ مَرَّةً ثَانِيَةً؟ فَاحْتَجَّ تَعَالَى عَلَيْهِمْ، وَنَبَّهَهُمْ عَلَى قُدْرَتِهِ عَلَى ذَلِكَ، بِأَنَّهُ خَلَقَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضَ، فَقُدْرَتُهُ عَلَى إِعَادَتِهِمْ أَسْهَلُ مِنْ ذَلِكَ كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿لَخَلْقُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأَرْضِ أَكْبَرُ مِنْ خَلْقِ النَّاسِ﴾ [غَافِرٍ: ٥٧] وَقَالَ ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَرَوْا أَنَّ اللَّهَ الَّذِي خَلَقَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأَرْضَ وَلَمْ يَعْيَ بِخَلْقِهِنَّ بِقَادِرٍ عَلَى أَنْ يُحْيِيَ الْمَوْتَى بَلَى إِنَّهُ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ﴾ [الْأَحْقَافِ: ٣٣] وَقَالَ ﴿أَوَلَيْسَ الَّذِي خَلَقَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأَرْضَ بِقَادِرٍ عَلَى أَنْ يَخْلُقَ مِثْلَهُمْ بَلَى وَهُوَ الْخَلاقُ الْعَلِيمُ * إِنَّمَا أَمْرُهُ إِذَا أَرَادَ شَيْئًا أَنْ يَقُولَ لَهُ كُنْ فَيَكُونُ * فَسُبْحَانَ الَّذِي بِيَدِهِ مَلَكُوتُ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ وَإِلَيْهِ تُرْجَعُونَ﴾ [يس: ٨١، ٨٣] .

وَقَالَ هَاهُنَا: (أَوَلَمْ يَرَوْا أَنَّ اللَّهَ الَّذِي خَلَقَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضَ قَادِرٌ عَلَى أَنْ يَخْلُقَ مِثْلَهُمْ) أَيْ: يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ يُعِيدُ أَبْدَانَهُمْ وَيُنَشِّئُهُمْ نَشْأَةً أُخْرَى، وَيُعِيدُهُمْ كَمَا بَدَأَهُمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: (وَجَعَلَ لَهُمْ أَجَلا لَا رَيْبَ فِيهِ) أَيْ: جَعَلَ لِإِعَادَتِهِمْ وَإِقَامَتِهِمْ مِنْ قُبُورِهِمْ أَجَلًا مَضْرُوبًا وَمُدَّةً مُقَدَّرَةً لَا بُدَّ مِنَ انْقِضَائِهَا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا نُؤَخِّرُهُ إِلا لأَجَلٍ مَعْدُودٍ﴾ [هُودٍ: ١٠٤] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: (فَأَبَى الظَّالِمُونَ) أَيْ: بَعْدَ قِيَامِ الْحُجَّةِ عَلَيْهِمْ (إِلا كُفُورًا) إِلَّا تماديًا في باطلهم وضلالهم.

---

## 17:100-101 — verses 100-101 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says to His Messenger ﷺ: say to them, O Muhammad: if you, O people, possessed control over the treasuries of God, you would withhold for fear of spending.

Ibn Abbas and Qatadah said: that is, for fear of poverty, meaning for fear that you would exhaust them, even though they never run out and are never depleted, because this is part of your nature and disposition. This is why He said: {and man has ever been miserly}. Ibn Abbas and Qatadah said: that is, stingy and withholding. God the Exalted said: {Or have they a share of the dominion? Then indeed they would not give the people so much as the speck on a date stone} [al-Nisa: 53], meaning: if they had a share in God's dominion, they would not give anyone anything, not even the measure of a naqir (speck on a date stone). God the Exalted describes man as he is in himself, except for one whom God has granted success and guided, for stinginess, distress, and anxious impatience are characteristics of him, as the Exalted said: {Indeed, man was created anxious and impatient. When evil touches him, he is distressed, and when good touches him, he is withholding, except those who pray} [al-Ma'arij: 19-22]. There are many similar passages in the Noble Qur'an. This also points to His generosity, His bounty, and His beneficence. It has come in the two Sahihs: "The hand of God is full, and it does not diminish through spending. It pours forth continuously, night and day. Have you considered what He has spent since He created the heavens and the earth? Indeed it has not decreased what is in His right hand."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى لِرَسُولِهِ صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ وَسَلَامُهُ قُلْ لَهُمْ يَا مُحَمَّدُ: لَوْ أَنَّكُمْ -أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ -تَمْلِكُونَ التَّصَرُّفَ فِي خَزَائِنِ اللَّهِ، لَأَمْسَكْتُمْ خَشْيَةَ الْإِنْفَاقِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَقَتَادَةُ: أَيِ الْفَقْرِ أَيْ: خَشْيَةَ أَنْ تُذْهِبُوهَا ، مَعَ أَنَّهَا لَا تَفْرَغُ وَلَا تَنْفَدُ أَبَدًا؛ لِأَنَّ هَذَا مِنْ طِبَاعِكُمْ وَسَجَايَاكُمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: (وَكَانَ الإنْسَانُ قَتُورًا) قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَقَتَادَةُ : أَيْ بَخِيلًا مَنُوعًا. وَقَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَمْ لَهُمْ نَصِيبٌ مِنَ الْمُلْكِ فَإِذًا لَا يُؤْتُونَ النَّاسَ نَقِيرًا﴾ [النِّسَاءِ: ٥٣] أَيْ: لَوْ أَنَّ لَهُمْ نَصِيبًا فِي مُلْكِ اللَّهِ لَمَا أَعْطَوْا أَحَدًا شَيْئًا، وَلَا مِقْدَارَ نَقِيرٍ، وَاللَّهُ تَعَالَى يَصِفُ الْإِنْسَانَ مِنْ حَيْثُ هُوَ، إِلَّا مَنْ وَفَّقَهُ اللَّهُ وَهَدَاهُ؛ فَإِنَّ الْبُخْلَ وَالْجَزَعَ وَالْهَلَعَ صِفَةٌ لَهُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّ الإِنْسَانَ خُلِقَ هَلُوعًا * إِذَا مَسَّهُ الشَّرُّ جَزُوعًا * وَإِذَا مَسَّهُ الْخَيْرُ مَنُوعًا * إِلا الْمُصَلِّينَ﴾ [الْمَعَارِجِ: ١٩ -٢٢] . وَلِهَذَا نَظَائِرُ كَثِيرَةٌ فِي الْقُرْآنِ الْعَزِيزِ، وَيَدُلُّ هَذَا عَلَى كَرَمِهِ وَجُودِهِ وَإِحْسَانِهِ، وَقَدْ جَاءَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ: "يَدُ اللَّهِ مَلْأَى لَا يَغيضُها نَفَقَةٌ، سَحَّاءُ اللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ، أَرَأَيْتُمْ مَا أَنْفَقَ مُنْذُ خَلَقَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضَ فَإِنَّهُ لَمْ يَغض مَا فِي يَمِينِهِ" .

---

## 17:102-104 — verses 102-104 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs us that He sent Musa with nine clear signs, which are the decisive proofs of the soundness of his prophethood and his truthfulness in what he conveyed on behalf of the One who sent him to Pharaoh. These are: the staff, the hand, the years (of drought), the sea, the flood, the locusts, the lice, the frogs, and the blood, detailed signs. This is what Ibn Abbas said.

Muhammad ibn Ka'b said: they are the hand, the staff, the five mentioned in Surat al-A'raf, the effacement (of the sorcerers' eyes or similar), and the stone.

It is also said, by Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, Ikrimah, al-Sha'bi, and Qatadah: they are his hand, his staff, the years, the diminishing of fruits, the flood, the locusts, the lice, the frogs, and the blood.

This view is apparent, clear, sound, and strong. Al-Hasan al-Basri combined "the years" and "the diminishing of fruits" into one, and held that the ninth was the staff swallowing what they had fabricated. {So they were arrogant and were a criminal people} [al-A'raf: 133], meaning: despite these signs and their witnessing of them, they disbelieved in them and denied them, while their own selves were certain of them, out of injustice and arrogance, and the signs did not benefit them. Likewise, if We had answered those who asked of you, O Prophet, what they asked, saying: {We will not believe in you until you make a spring gush forth for us from the earth} [al-Isra: 90] to the end of the verse, they would not have responded nor believed, except by the will of Allah. This is as Pharaoh said to Musa, after having witnessed what he witnessed of these signs: "Indeed, I think you, O Musa, are bewitched (mashur)," which is said to mean "a sorcerer." And Allah knows best.

These nine signs mentioned by these leading scholars are what is intended here, and they are what is meant in His statement: {And cast down your staff. Then when he saw it moving as if it were a snake, he turned in flight and did not return. O Musa, do not fear. Indeed, the messengers do not fear in My presence, except one who has done wrong, then substitutes good for evil, for indeed I am forgiving and merciful. And put your hand into your bosom, it will come out white without any harm, among nine signs to Pharaoh and his people. Indeed, they were a rebellious people} [al-Naml: 10-12]. Here He mentioned these two signs, the staff and the hand, and He detailed the remaining signs in Surat al-A'raf, spelling them out in full.

Musa (peace be upon him) was given many other signs besides these, among them his striking the rock with his staff and the springing forth of rivers from it, his people's being shaded by the cloud, and the sending down of manna and quails, and other things that the Children of Israel were given after their departure from the land of Egypt. But what is mentioned here are the nine signs which Pharaoh and his people, the people of Egypt, witnessed, and which stood as a proof against them, yet they opposed them and defied them out of disbelief and denial.

As for the hadith reported by the Imam [Ahmad]:

[chain] Yazid told us, Shu'bah told us, from Amr ibn Murrah, who said: I heard Abdullah ibn Salamah relate, from Safwan ibn Assal al-Muradi, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: A Jew said to his companion: Let us go to this prophet [ﷺ] so that we may ask him about this verse: {And indeed We gave Musa nine clear signs}. He said: Do not call him "prophet," for if he hears you, he will grow four eyes. So they asked him, and the Prophet ﷺ said: "Do not associate anything with Allah, do not steal, do not commit adultery, do not kill the soul which Allah has forbidden except by right, do not practice sorcery, do not consume usury, do not walk with an innocent man toward a ruler in order to have him killed, and do not accuse a chaste woman of unchastity, or he said: do not flee from the battle line (Shu'bah was uncertain), and you, O Jews, are specifically required not to transgress on the Sabbath." So the two of them kissed his hands and feet and said: We bear witness that you are a prophet. [He said: "What prevents you two from following me?" They said: Because Dawud (peace be upon him) prayed that there would always be a prophet among his descendants], and we fear that if we submit, the Jews will kill us.

This hadith was related in this manner by al-Tirmidhi, al-Nasa'i, Ibn Majah, and Ibn Jarir in his tafsir, through routes from Shu'bah ibn al-Hajjaj, with this wording. Al-Tirmidhi said: hasan sahih (sound and authentic).

But it is a problematic hadith, and Abdullah ibn Salamah's memory had some issue, scholars have spoken critically of him. Perhaps he confused the nine signs with the ten commandments, for these are injunctions in the Torah with no connection to establishing proof against Pharaoh. And Allah knows best.

For this reason Musa said to Pharaoh: {You have certainly known that none has sent down these except the Lord of the heavens and the earth, as insights}, meaning: proofs and evidences of the truth of what I have brought you, {and indeed I think you, O Pharaoh, are doomed (mathbura)}, meaning: destroyed. This is what Mujahid and Qatadah said. Ibn Abbas said it means "cursed." He and al-Dahhak also said "mathbura" means "overcome." And "destroyed," as Mujahid said, encompasses all of this. Abdullah ibn al-Zib'ara said:

"When I accompany Satan on the path of error, whoever inclines toward his inclination is doomed (mathbur)" [meaning destroyed].

Some read the ta in "'alimtu" with the raf' (nominative-like) vowel ending, and this was related from Ali ibn Abi Talib. But the reading of the majority is with the fatha on the ta, addressing Pharaoh directly, as the Almighty said: {And when Our signs came to them, visible, they said, "This is clear sorcery." And they rejected them while their own souls were certain of them, out of injustice and arrogance. So see how was the end of the corrupters} [al-Naml: 13-14].

All of this points to the fact that what is meant by the nine signs is what has already been mentioned: the staff, the hand, the years, the diminishing of fruits, the flood, the locusts, the lice, the frogs, and the blood. These contain proofs and demonstrations against Pharaoh and his people, and extraordinary signs and evidences of the truthfulness of Musa and the existence of the free-acting Agent who sent him. What is meant is not what is found in this hadith, for these injunctions contain no proofs against Pharaoh and his people, and what relation is there between this and the establishing of proofs against Pharaoh? This confusion has come only from Abdullah ibn Salamah, for he has some reports that are considered objectionable. And Allah knows best. Perhaps those two Jews had only asked about the ten commandments, and the narrator confused this with the nine signs, and thus a mistake occurred in this. And Allah knows best.

And His statement: {So he intended to uproot them from the land}, meaning: to empty them out of it and remove them from it, {so We drowned him and those with him, all together. And We said after him to the Children of Israel: dwell in the land}. In this there is glad tidings for Muhammad ﷺ of the conquest of Mecca, even though this surah was revealed before the Hijrah, and this is indeed what happened, for the people of Mecca intended to expel the Messenger from it, as the Almighty said: {And indeed they were about to unsettle you from the land to expel you from it, and then they would not have remained after you except for a little while. That is the way of those We sent before you of Our messengers, and you will not find in Our way any alteration} [al-Isra: 76-77]. For this reason Allah caused His Messenger to inherit Mecca, and he entered it by conquest, according to the more well-known of the two views, and he overpowered its people, then released them out of forbearance and generosity, just as Allah caused the people who had been oppressed among the Children of Israel to inherit the easts and wests of the earth, and caused them to inherit the lands of Pharaoh and their wealth, their crops, their fruits, and their treasures, as He said: {Thus, and We caused the Children of Israel to inherit it} [al-Shu'ara: 59]. And He said here: {And We said after him to the Children of Israel: dwell in the land, and when the promise of the Hereafter comes, We will bring you all together, mixed together}, meaning: all of you, you and your enemies together.

Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, Qatadah, and al-Dahhak said: "lafifan" means "all together."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ بَعَثَ مُوسَى بِتِسْعِ آيَاتٍ بَيِّنَاتٍ، وَهِيَ الدَّلَائِلُ الْقَاطِعَةُ عَلَى صِحَّةِ نُبُوَّتِهِ وَصِدْقِهِ فِيمَا أَخْبَرَ بِهِ عَمَّنْ أَرْسَلَهُ إِلَى فِرْعَوْنَ، وَهِيَ: الْعَصَا، وَالْيَدُ، وَالسِّنِينَ ، وَالْبَحْرُ، وَالطُّوفَانُ ، وَالْجَرَادُ، وَالْقُمَّلُ، وَالضَّفَادِعُ، وَالدَّمُ، آيَاتٍ مُفَصَّلَاتٍ. قَالَهُ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ: هِيَ الْيَدُ، وَالْعَصَا، وَالْخَمْسُ فِي الْأَعْرَافِ، والطَّمْسَة وَالْحَجَرُ.

وَقَالَ: ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ أَيْضًا، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ وَالشَّعْبِيُّ، وَقَتَادَةُ: هِيَ يَدُهُ، وَعَصَاهُ، وَالسِّنِينَ، وَنَقْصُ الثَّمَرَاتِ، وَالطُّوفَانُ، وَالْجَرَادُ، وَالْقُمَّلُ، وَالضَّفَادِعُ، وَالدَّمُ.

وَهَذَا الْقَوْلُ ظَاهِرٌ جَلِيٌّ حَسَنٌ قَوِيٌّ. وَجَعَلَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ "السِّنِينَ وَنَقْصَ الثَّمَرَاتِ" وَاحِدَةً، وَعِنْدَهُ أَنَّ التَّاسِعَةَ هِيَ: تَلَقُّفُ الْعَصَا مَا يَأْفِكُونَ. ﴿فَاسْتَكْبَرُوا وَكَانُوا قَوْمًا مُجْرِمِينَ﴾ [الأعراف: ١٣٣] أَيْ: وَمَعَ هَذِهِ الْآيَاتِ وَمُشَاهَدَتِهِمْ لَهَا، كَفَرُوا بِهَا وَجَحَدُوا بِهَا، وَاسْتَيْقَنَتْهَا أَنْفُسُهُمْ ظُلْمًا وَعُلُوًّا، وَمَا نَجَعَتْ فِيهِمْ، فَكَذَلِكَ لَوْ أَجَبْنَا هَؤُلَاءِ الَّذِينَ سَأَلُوا مِنْكَ سَأَلُوا، وَقَالُوا: ﴿لَنْ نُؤْمِنَ لَكَ حَتَّى تَفْجُرَ لَنَا مِنَ الأَرْضِ يَنْبُوعًا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٩٠] إِلَى آخِرِهَا، لَمَا اسْتَجَابُوا وَلَا آمَنُوا إِلَّا أَنْ يَشَاءَ اللَّهُ، كَمَا قَالَ فِرْعَوْنُ لِمُوسَى -وَقَدْ شَاهَدَ مِنْهُ مَا شَاهَدَ مِنْ هذه الآيات-: (إِنِّي لأظُنُّكَ يَا مُوسَى مَسْحُورًا) قِيلَ: بِمَعْنَى سَاحِرٍ. وَاللَّهُ تَعَالَى أَعْلَمُ.

فَهَذِهِ الْآيَاتُ التِّسْعُ الَّتِي ذَكَرَهَا هَؤُلَاءِ الْأَئِمَّةُ هِيَ الْمُرَادَةُ هَاهُنَا، وَهِيَ الْمَعْنِيَّةُ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَأَلْقِ عَصَاكَ فَلَمَّا رَآهَا تَهْتَزُّ كَأَنَّهَا جَانٌّ وَلَّى مُدْبِرًا وَلَمْ يُعَقِّبْ يَا مُوسَى لَا تَخَفْ إِنِّي لَا يَخَافُ لَدَيَّ الْمُرْسَلُونَ * إِلا مَنْ ظَلَمَ ثُمَّ بَدَّلَ حُسْنًا بَعْدَ سُوءٍ فَإِنِّي غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ * وَأَدْخِلْ يَدَكَ فِي جَيْبِكَ تَخْرُجْ بَيْضَاءَ مِنْ غَيْرِ سُوءٍ فِي تِسْعِ آيَاتٍ إِلَى فِرْعَوْنَ وَقَوْمِهِ إِنَّهُمْ كَانُوا قَوْمًا فَاسِقِينَ﴾ [النَّمْلِ: ١٠ -١٢] . فَذَكَرَ هَاتَيْنِ الْآيَتَيْنِ: الْعَصَا وَالْيَدَ، وَبَيَّنَ الْآيَاتِ الْبَاقِيَاتِ فِي "سُورَةِ الْأَعْرَافِ" وَفَصَّلَهَا.

وَقَدْ أُوتِيَ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، آيَاتٍ أخرَ كَثِيرَةً، مِنْهَا ضربُه الْحَجَرَ بِالْعَصَا، وَخُرُوجُ الْأَنْهَارِ مِنْهُ، وَمِنْهَا تَظْلِيلُهُمْ بِالْغَمَامِ، وَإِنْزَالُ الْمَنِّ وَالسَّلْوَى، وَغَيْرُ ذَلِكَ مِمَّا أُوتُوهُ بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ بَعْدَ مُفَارَقَتِهِمْ بِلَادَ مِصْرَ، وَلَكِنْ ذَكَرَ هَاهُنَا التِّسْعَ الْآيَاتِ الَّتِي شَاهَدَهَا فِرْعَوْنُ وَقَوْمُهُ مِنْ أَهْلِ مِصْرَ، وَكَانَتْ حُجَّةً عَلَيْهِمْ فَخَالَفُوهَا وَعَانَدُوهَا كُفْرًا وَجُحُودًا. فَأَمَّا الْحَدِيثُ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ [أَحْمَدُ] :

حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ مُرَّة قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ سَلَمَةَ يُحَدِّثُ، عَنْ صَفْوَانَ بْنِ عَسّال الْمُرَادِيِّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ يَهُودِيٌّ لِصَاحِبِهِ: اذْهَبْ بِنَا إِلَى هَذَا النَّبِيِّ [ﷺ] حَتَّى نَسْأَلَهُ عَنْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: (وَلَقَدْ آتَيْنَا مُوسَى تِسْعَ آيَاتٍ بَيِّنَاتٍ) فَقَالَ: لَا تَقُلْ لَهُ: نَبِيٌّ فَإِنَّهُ لَوْ سَمِعَكَ لَصَارَتْ لَهُ أَرْبَعُ أَعْيُنٍ. فَسَأَلَاهُ، فَقَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "لَا تُشْرِكُوا بِاللَّهِ شَيْئًا، وَلَا تَسْرِقُوا، وَلَا تَزْنُوا، وَلَا تَقْتُلُوا النَّفْسَ الَّتِي حَرَّمَ اللَّهُ إِلَّا بِالْحَقِّ، وَلَا تَسْحَرُوا، وَلَا تَأْكُلُوا الرِّبَا، وَلَا تَمْشُوا بِبَرِيءٍ إِلَى ذِي سُلْطَانٍ لِيَقْتُلَهُ، وَلَا تَقْذِفُوا مُحْصَنَةً -أَوْ قَالَ: لَا تَفِرُّوا مِنَ الزَّحْفِ -شُعْبَةُ الشَّاكُّ -وَأَنْتُمْ يَا يَهُودُ، عَلَيْكُمْ خَاصَّةً أَنْ لَا تَعْدُوا فِي السَّبْتِ". فَقَبَّلَا يَدَيْهِ وَرِجْلَيْهِ، وَقَالَا نَشْهَدُ أَنَّكَ نَبِيٌّ. [قَالَ: "فَمَا يَمْنَعُكُمَا أَنْ تَتَّبِعَانِي؟ " قَالَا لِأَنَّ دَاوُدَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، دَعَا أَلَّا يَزَالَ مِنْ ذُرِّيَّتِهِ نَبِيٌّ] ، وَإِنَّا نَخْشَى إِنْ أَسْلَمْنَا أَنْ تَقْتُلَنَا يَهُودُ.

فَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ رَوَاهُ هَكَذَا التِّرْمِذِيُّ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ، وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ، وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ مِنْ طُرُقٍ عَنْ شُعْبَةَ بْنِ الْحَجَّاجِ، بِهِ وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ.

وَهُوَ حَدِيثُ مُشْكَلٌ، وَعَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ فِي حِفْظِهِ شَيْءٌ، وَقَدْ تَكَلَّمُوا فِيهِ، وَلَعَلَّهُ اشْتَبَهَ عَلَيْهِ التِّسْعُ الْآيَاتُ بِالْعَشْرِ الْكَلِمَاتِ، فَإِنَّهَا، وَصَايَا فِي التَّوْرَاةِ لَا تَعَلُّقَ لَهَا بقيام الحجة على فرعون، والله أعلم.

وَلِهَذَا قَالَ مُوسَى لِفِرْعَوْنَ: (لَقَدْ عَلِمْتَ مَا أَنزلَ هَؤُلاءِ إِلا رَبُّ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ بَصَائِرَ) أَيْ: حُجَجًا وَأَدِلَّةً عَلَى صِدْقِ مَا جِئْتُكَ به (وَإِنِّي لأظُنُّكَ يَا فِرْعَوْنُ مَثْبُورًا) أَيْ: هَالِكًا. قَالَهُ مُجَاهِدٌ وَقَتَادَةُ. وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ مَلْعُونًا. وَقَالَ: أَيْضًا هُوَ وَالضَّحَّاكُ: (مَثْبُورًا) أَيْ: مَغْلُوبًا. وَالْهَالِكُ -كَمَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ -يَشْمَلُ هَذَا كُلَّهُ، قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الزِّبَعْرَى:

إذْ أجَارِي الشَّيطانَ فِي سَنن الْغَـ ... يِّ وَمَنْ مَالَ مَيْلهُ مَثْبُور 

[بِمَعْنَى هَالِكٍ] .

وَقَرَأَ بَعْضُهُمْ بِرَفْعِ التَّاءِ مِنْ قَوْلِهِ: "عَلِمْتُ" وَرُوِيَ ذَلِكَ عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ أَبِي طَالِبٍ. وَلَكِنْ قِرَاءَةَ الْجُمْهُورِ بِفَتْحِ التَّاءِ عَلَى الْخِطَابِ لِفِرْعَوْنَ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَلَمَّا جَاءَتْهُمْ آيَاتُنَا مُبْصِرَةً قَالُوا هَذَا سِحْرٌ مُبِينٌ * وَجَحَدُوا بِهَا وَاسْتَيْقَنَتْهَا أَنْفُسُهُمْ ظُلْمًا وَعُلُوًّا فَانْظُرْ كَيْفَ كَانَ عَاقِبَةُ الْمُفْسِدِينَ﴾ [النَّمْلِ: ١٣، ١٤] .

فَهَذَا كُلُّهُ مِمَّا يَدُلُّ عَلَى أَنَّ الْمُرَادَ بِالتِّسْعِ الْآيَاتِ إِنَّمَا هِيَ مَا تَقَدَّمَ ذِكْرُهُ مِنَ الْعَصَا، وَالْيَدِ، وَالسِّنِينَ، وَنَقْصٍ مِنَ الثَّمَرَاتِ، وَالطُّوفَانِ، وَالْجَرَادِ، والقُمَّل، وَالضَّفَادِعِ، وَالدَّمِ. الَّتِي فِيهَا حُجَجٌ وَبَرَاهِينُ عَلَى فِرْعَوْنَ وَقَوْمِهِ، وَخَوَارِقُ وَدَلَائِلُ عَلَى صِدْقِ مُوسَى وَوُجُودِ الْفَاعِلِ الْمُخْتَارِ الَّذِي أَرْسَلَهُ. وَلَيْسَ الْمُرَادُ مِنْهَا كَمَا وَرَدَ فِي هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ، فَإِنَّ هَذِهِ الْوَصَايَا لَيْسَ فِيهَا حُجَجٌ عَلَى فِرْعَوْنَ وَقَوْمِهِ، وَأَيُّ مُنَاسَبَةٍ بَيْنَ هَذَا وَبَيْنَ إِقَامَةِ الْبَرَاهِينِ عَلَى فِرْعَوْنَ؟ وَمَا جَاءَ هَذَا الْوَهْمُ إِلَّا مِنْ قِبَلِ "عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ سَلَمَةَ فَإِنَّ لَهُ بَعْضَ مَا يُنْكر. وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ. وَلَعَلَّ ذَيْنِكَ الْيَهُودِيَّيْنِ إِنَّمَا سَأَلَا عَنِ الْعَشْرِ الْكَلِمَاتِ، فَاشْتَبَهَ عَلَى الرَّاوِي بِالتِّسْعِ الْآيَاتِ، فَحَصَلَ وَهْم فِي ذَلِكَ. وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: (فَأَرَادَ أَنْ يَسْتَفِزَّهُمْ مِنَ الأرْضِ) أَيْ: يُخْلِيَهُمْ مِنْهَا وَيُزِيلَهُمْ عَنْهَا (فَأَغْرَقْنَاهُ وَمَنْ مَعَهُ جَمِيعًا * وَقُلْنَا مِنْ بَعْدِهِ لِبَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ اسْكُنُوا الأرْضَ) وَفِي هَذَا بِشَارَةٌ لِمُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ بِفَتْحِ مَكَّةَ مَعَ أَنَّ السُّورَةَ نَزَلَتْ قَبْلَ الْهِجْرَةِ، وَكَذَلِكَ وَقَعَ؛ فَإِنَّ أَهْلَ مَكَّةَ هَمُّوا بِإِخْرَاجِ الرَّسُولِ مِنْهَا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِنْ كَادُوا لَيَسْتَفِزُّونَكَ مِنَ الأَرْضِ لِيُخْرِجُوكَ مِنْهَا وَإِذًا لَا يَلْبَثُونَ خِلافَكَ إِلا قَلِيلا * سُنَّةَ مَنْ قَدْ أَرْسَلْنَا قَبْلَكَ مِنْ رُسُلِنَا وَلا تَجِدُ لِسُنَّتِنَا تَحْوِيلا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٧٦، ٧٧] ؛ وَلِهَذَا أَوْرَثَ اللَّهُ رَسُولَهُ مَكَّةَ، فَدَخَلَهَا عُنْوَة عَلَى أَشْهَرِ الْقَوْلَيْنِ، وَقَهَرَ أَهْلَهَا، ثُمَّ أَطْلَقَهُمْ حِلْمًا وَكَرَمًا، كَمَا أَوْرَثَ اللَّهُ الْقَوْمَ الَّذِينَ كَانُوا يُسْتَضْعَفُونَ مِنْ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ مَشَارِقَ الْأَرْضِ وَمَغَارِبَهَا، وَأَوْرَثَهُمْ بِلَادَ فِرْعَوْنَ وَأَمْوَالَهُمْ وزروعهم وَثِمَارَهُمْ وَكُنُوزَهُمْ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿كَذَلِكَ وَأَوْرَثْنَاهَا بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ﴾ [الشُّعَرَاءِ: ٥٩] وَقَالَ هَاهُنَا (وَقُلْنَا مِنْ بَعْدِهِ لِبَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ اسْكُنُوا الأرْضَ فَإِذَا جَاءَ وَعْدُ الآخِرَةِ جِئْنَا بِكُمْ لَفِيفًا) أَيْ: جَمِيعُكُمْ أَنْتُمْ وَعَدُوُّكُمْ.

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ وَمُجَاهِدٌ وَقَتَادَةُ وَالضَّحَّاكُ: (لَفِيفًا) أَيْ: جَمِيعًا.

---

## 17:105-106 — verses 105-106 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted informs about His Mighty Book, which is the glorious Qur'an, that it descended with truth, meaning it contains and comprises truth, as He, the Exalted, said: {But God bears witness by what He has sent down to you, He sent it down with His knowledge} [al-Nisa: 166], meaning it comprises the knowledge of God which He willed to disclose to you, from His rulings, His commands, and His prohibitions.

Regarding His saying, {and with truth it descended}, meaning: it reached you, O Muhammad, preserved and guarded, unmixed with anything else, nothing added to it and nothing removed from it. Rather it reached you with truth, for it was brought down by the one of mighty powers, the strong one, the trustworthy, the firmly established, the one obeyed in the highest assembly (al-mala' al-a'la).

Regarding His saying, {And We have not sent you}, meaning: O Muhammad, {except as a bringer of good tidings} to those among the believers who obey you, {and a warner} to those among the disbelievers who disobey you.

Regarding His saying, {and a Qur'an which We have divided}: as for the reading of those who read it with the light form (takhfif), its meaning is: We separated it out from al-Lawh al-Mahfuz (the Preserved Tablet) to Bayt al-'Izzah in the lowest heaven, and then it descended divided into portions, in accordance with events, to the Messenger of God ﷺ over twenty-three years. This was said by 'Ikrimah, from Ibn 'Abbas.

And it is also related from Ibn 'Abbas that he read {farraqnahu} with the heavy form (tashdid), meaning: We sent it down verse by verse, made clear and explained. This is why He said: {so that you may recite it to the people} meaning: so that you may convey it to the people and recite it to them, {at intervals}, meaning: gradually, with pauses, {and We sent it down progressively}, meaning: bit by bit, one part after another.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ كِتَابِهِ الْعَزِيزِ، وَهُوَ الْقُرْآنُ الْمَجِيدُ، أَنَّهُ بِالْحَقِّ نَزَلَ، أَيْ: مُتَضَمِّنًا لِلْحَقِّ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَكِنِ اللَّهُ يَشْهَدُ بِمَا أَنزلَ إِلَيْكَ أَنزلَهُ بِعِلْمِهِ﴾ [النِّسَاءِ: ١٦٦] أَيْ: مُتَضَمِّنًا عِلْمَ اللَّهِ الَّذِي أَرَادَ أَنْ يُطْلِعكم عَلَيْهِ، مِنْ أَحْكَامِهِ وَأَمْرِهِ وَنَهْيِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَبِالْحَقِّ نزلَ﴾ أَيْ: وَوَصَلَ إِلَيْكَ -يَا مُحَمَّدُ -مَحْفُوظًا مَحْرُوسًا، لَمْ يُشَب بِغَيْرِهِ، وَلَا زِيدَ فِيهِ وَلَا نُقص مِنْهُ، بَلْ وَصَلَ إِلَيْكَ بِالْحَقِّ، فَإِنَّهُ نَزَلَ بِهِ شَدِيدُ القُوى، [القَوِيّ] الْأَمِينُ الْمَكِينُ الْمُطَاعُ فِي الْمَلَإِ الْأَعْلَى.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا أَرْسَلْنَاكَ﴾ أَيْ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ ﴿إِلا مُبَشِّرًا﴾ لِمَنْ أَطَاعَكَ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ ﴿وَنَذِيرًا﴾ لِمَنْ عَصَاكَ مِنَ الْكَافِرِينَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَقُرْآنًا فَرَقْنَاهُ﴾ أَمَّا قِرَاءَةُ مَنْ قَرَأَ بِالتَّخْفِيفِ، فَمَعْنَاهُ: فَصَّلْنَاهُ مِنَ اللَّوْحِ الْمَحْفُوظِ إِلَى بَيْتِ الْعِزَّةِ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ الدُّنْيَا، ثُمَّ نَزَلَ مُفرقًا مُنَجَّمًا عَلَى الْوَقَائِعِ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فِي ثَلَاثٍ وَعِشْرِينَ سَنَةً. قَالَهُ عِكْرِمَةُ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ.

وَعَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ أَيْضًا أَنَّهُ قَالَ ﴿فَرَقْنَاهُ﴾ بِالتَّشْدِيدِ، أَيْ: أَنْزَلْنَاهُ آيَةً آيَةً، مُبَيَّنًا مُفَسَّرًا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿لِتَقْرَأَهُ عَلَى النَّاسِ﴾ أَيْ: لِتُبَلِّغَهُ النَّاسَ وَتَتْلُوهُ عَلَيْهِمْ ﴿عَلَى مُكْثٍ﴾ أَيْ: مَهَل ﴿وَنزلْنَاهُ تَنزيلا﴾ أَيْ: شَيْئًا بَعْدَ شَيْءٍ.

---

## 17:107-109 — verses 107-109 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says to His Prophet Muhammad ﷺ: {Say} O Muhammad, to these disbelievers regarding what you have brought them of this magnificent Qur'an: {believe in it or do not believe} meaning: whether you believe in it or not, it is true in itself, God has sent it down and made mention of it in bygone times in the books He revealed to His messengers. Therefore He says: {Indeed, those who were given knowledge before it} meaning: among the righteous People of the Book who hold fast to their book and uphold it, and did not alter it or distort it, {when it is recited to them}, meaning this Qur'an, {they fall down on their chins}, "adhqan" being the plural of "dhaqn," which is the lower part of the face, {in prostration}, meaning: to God, Mighty and Majestic, in gratitude for the favor He bestowed upon them by making them fit to have reached this Messenger upon whom [this] Book was sent down. Therefore they say: {Glory be to our Lord}, meaning: in exaltation and reverence for His complete power, and that He does not break the promise which He gave them through the tongues of the earlier prophets [who preceded the mission of Muhammad ﷺ. Therefore they said: {Glory be to our Lord, indeed the promise of our Lord is to be fulfilled}].

His statement: {and they fall down on their chins weeping} means: in submission to God, Mighty and Majestic, and in faith and confirmation of His Book and His Messenger, and God increases them in humility, meaning: in faith and submission, as He said: {And those who are guided, He increases them in guidance and gives them their righteousness} [Muhammad: 17].

His statement: {and they fall down} is a conjunction of one description upon another description, not a conjunction of one act of prostration upon another act of prostration, as the poet said:

To the noble king, son of the valiant chief... and the lion of the battalion amid the throng...

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى لِنَبِيِّهِ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ: ﴿قُلْ﴾ يَا مُحَمَّدُ لِهَؤُلَاءِ الْكَافِرِينَ بِمَا جِئْتَهُمْ بِهِ مِنْ هَذَا الْقُرْآنِ الْعَظِيمِ: ﴿آمِنُوا بِهِ أَوْ لَا تُؤْمِنُوا﴾ أَيْ: سَوَاءٌ آمَنْتُمْ بِهِ أَمْ لَا فَهُوَ حَقٌّ فِي نَفْسِهِ، أَنْزَلَهُ اللَّهُ وَنَوَّهَ بِذِكْرِهِ فِي سَالِفِ الْأَزْمَانِ فِي كُتُبِهِ الْمُنَزَّلَةِ عَلَى رُسُلِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْعِلْمَ مِنْ قَبْلِهِ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ صَالِحِ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ الَّذِينَ يُمَسَّكون بِكِتَابِهِمْ وَيُقِيمُونَهُ، وَلَمْ يُبَدِّلُوهُ وَلَا حَرَّفُوهُ ﴿إِذَا يُتْلَى عَلَيْهِمْ﴾ هذا الْقُرْآنُ، ﴿يَخِرُّونَ لِلأذْقَانِ﴾ جَمْعُ ذَقْن، وَهُوَ أَسْفَلُ الْوَجْهِ ﴿سُجَّدًا﴾ أَيْ: لِلَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، شُكْرًا عَلَى مَا أَنْعَمَ بِهِ عَلَيْهِمْ، مِنْ جَعْلِهِ إِيَّاهُمْ أَهْلًا إِنْ أَدْرَكُوا هَذَا الرَّسُولَ الَّذِي أُنْزِلَ عَلَيْهِ [هَذَا] الْكِتَابُ؛ وَلِهَذَا يَقُولُونَ: ﴿سُبْحَانَ رَبِّنَا﴾ أَيْ: تَعْظِيمًا وَتَوْقِيرًا عَلَى قُدْرَتِهِ التَّامَّةِ، وَأَنَّهُ لَا يُخْلِفُ الْمِيعَادَ الَّذِي وَعَدَهُمْ عَلَى أَلْسِنَةِ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ [الْمُتَقَدِّمِينَ عَنْ بَعْثَةِ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالُوا: ﴿سُبْحَانَ رَبِّنَا إِنْ كَانَ وَعْدُ رَبِّنَا لَمَفْعُولا﴾ ] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَيَخِرُّونَ لِلأذْقَانِ يَبْكُونَ﴾ أَيْ: خُضُوعًا لِلَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ وَإِيمَانًا وَتَصْدِيقًا بِكِتَابِهِ وَرَسُولِهِ، وَيَزِيدُهُمُ اللَّهُ خُشُوعًا، أَيْ: إِيمَانًا وَتَسْلِيمًا كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ اهْتَدَوْا زَادَهُمْ هُدًى وَآتَاهُمْ تَقْوَاهُمْ﴾ [مُحَمَّدٍ: ١٧] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَيَخِرُّونَ﴾ عَطْفُ صِفَةٍ عَلَى صِفَةٍ لَا عَطْفُ سُجُودٍ عَلَى سُجُودٍ، كَمَا قَالَ الشَّاعِرُ:

إلَى المَلك القَرْم وَابْنِ الهُمام ... وَلَيْث الكَتِيبَة في المُزْدَحَمْ ...

---

## 17:110-111 — verses 110-111 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: Say, O Muhammad, to these polytheists who deny the attribute of mercy for Allah, exalted and glorified, and who forbid naming Him "al-Rahman": {Say: "Call upon Allah or call upon al-Rahman: whichever you call upon, to Him belong the most beautiful names."} That is, there is no difference between your calling upon Him by the name "Allah" or by the name "al-Rahman," for He possesses the most beautiful names, as the Almighty said: {He is Allah, besides whom there is no god, Knower of the unseen and the witnessed. He is al-Rahman, al-Rahim} up to where He said: {To Him belong the most beautiful names. Whatever is in the heavens and the earth glorifies Him, and He is the Mighty, the Wise} [al-Hashr: 22-24].

Makhul narrated that a man among the polytheists heard the Prophet ﷺ saying in his prostration, "O Rahman, O Rahim," and said: he claims he is calling upon one, yet he is calling upon two. So Allah revealed this verse. The same has been narrated from Ibn Abbas; both reports were narrated by Ibn Jarir.

Regarding His saying, {And do not be loud in your prayer} the verse, Imam Ahmad said:

[chain] Hushaym told us, Abu Bishr told us, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, who said: this verse was revealed while he was in hiding in Mecca, {And do not be loud in your prayer, nor say it in a low voice, [but seek a way between that]}. He said: when he prayed with his companions he would raise his voice with the Qur'an, and when the polytheists heard that, they would curse the Qur'an and curse the One who sent it down and the one who brought it. He said: so Allah, exalted, said to His Prophet ﷺ: {And do not be loud in your prayer}, meaning your recitation, lest the polytheists hear it and curse the Qur'an, {nor say it in a low voice}, meaning before your companions, so that you do not make them unable to hear the Qur'an so that they may take it from you, {but seek a way between that}.

Both Bukhari and Muslim narrated it from the hadith of Abu Bishr Ja'far ibn Iyas, with this chain. Al-Dahhak likewise narrated it from Ibn Abbas, and added: "Then when he emigrated to Medina, that requirement lapsed, and he would do whichever of the two he wished."

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: Dawud ibn al-Husayn told me, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas, who said: When the Messenger of Allah ﷺ was loud with the Qur'an while praying, they would scatter away from him and refuse to listen to him. So if a man wanted to hear some of what he recited while he was praying, he would steal a listen apart from them out of fear of them. If he saw that they had realized he was listening, he would leave for fear of their harming him, and so would not listen. But if the Prophet ﷺ lowered his voice, those who were trying to listen to his recitation would not hear anything at all. So Allah revealed: {And do not be loud in your prayer}, lest they scatter away from you, {nor say it in a low voice}, so that you do not prevent someone who wants to hear it, among those stealing a listen apart from the others, from hearing it, so that perhaps he might take heed of some of what he hears and benefit from it, {but seek a way between that}.

Ikrimah, al-Hasan al-Basri, and Qatadah likewise said: this verse was revealed concerning recitation in prayer.

Shu'bah said, from Ash'ath ibn Abi Sulaym, from al-Aswad ibn Hilal, from Ibn Mas'ud: one who makes his own ears hear it has not spoken in a low voice.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Ya'qub told us, Ibn Ulayyah told us, from Salamah ibn Alqamah, from Muhammad ibn Sirin, who said: I was informed that Abu Bakr, when he prayed and recited, would lower his voice, and that Umar would raise his voice. So it was said to Abu Bakr: why do you do this? He said: I am conversing intimately with my Lord, exalted and glorified, and He already knows my need. It was said: you have done well. And it was said to Umar: why do you do this? He said: I drive away Satan, and I wake the drowsy. It was said: you have done well. Then when {And do not be loud in your prayer, nor say it in a low voice, but seek a way between that} was revealed, it was said to Abu Bakr: raise it somewhat, and it was said to Umar: lower it somewhat.

Ash'ath ibn Sawwar said, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas: it was revealed concerning supplication (du'a). Likewise al-Thawri and Malik narrated, from Hisham ibn Urwah, from his father, from Aisha: it was revealed concerning supplication. Mujahid, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Abu Iyad, Makhul, and Urwah ibn al-Zubayr said the same.

Al-Thawri said, from [Ibn] Ayyash al-Amiri, from Abdullah ibn Shaddad, who said: there were bedouin of Banu Tamim who, when the Prophet ﷺ gave the closing salutation, would say: O Allah, provide us with camels and offspring. He said: so this verse was revealed: {And do not be loud in your prayer, nor say it in a low voice}.

Another view: Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Abu al-Sa'ib told us, Hafs ibn Ghiyath told us, from Hisham ibn Urwah, from his father, from Aisha, may Allah be pleased with her: this verse was revealed concerning the tashahhud: {And do not be loud in your prayer, nor say it in a low voice}.

And with the same chain, Hafs said, from Ash'ath ibn Sawwar, from Muhammad ibn Sirin, the same.

Another view: Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn Abbas, regarding His saying: {And do not be loud in your prayer, nor say it in a low voice}: do not pray to show off before people, nor abandon it out of fear of people. Al-Thawri said, from Mansur, from al-Hasan al-Basri: {And do not be loud in your prayer, nor say it in a low voice}, he said: do not make its outward appearance good while making its inward reality corrupt. Likewise Abd al-Razzaq narrated it, from Ma'mar, from al-Hasan, with this wording. And Hushaym, from Awf, from him, with this. And Sa'id, from Qatadah, from him, likewise.

Another view: Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said regarding His saying: {but seek a way between that}: the People of the Book speak in a low voice, then one of them raises his voice on a single letter and shouts it, and the others shout it after him. So he was forbidden to shout as these people shout, and to speak in a low voice as those people do, and rather the way between the two was that which Gabriel established for him regarding the prayer.

Regarding His saying: {And say: "Praise be to Allah, who has not taken a child"} when the Almighty affirmed for His noble Self the most beautiful names, He declared Himself free of deficiencies and said: {And say: "Praise be to Allah, who has not taken a child, nor has He a partner in dominion"} rather He is Allah, the One, al-Samad (the Self-Sufficient Master relied upon by all, free of need, sought by all in their needs), who has not begotten and was not begotten, and there is none comparable to Him.

{And He has no protector out of weakness}, meaning He is not lowly such that He would need a protector or a minister or an advisor. Rather He, exalted is His affair, is the Creator of all things alone, having no partner, and the One who determines and manages them by His will alone, having no partner.

Mujahid said regarding His saying: {And He has no protector out of weakness}: He has not allied with anyone, nor does He seek the aid of anyone.

{And magnify Him with great magnification}, meaning: glorify Him and exalt Him far above what the wrongdoers, the transgressors, say, with a great exaltation.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Yunus told me, Ibn Wahb informed us, Abu Sakhr told me, from al-Qurazi, that he used to say regarding this verse, {And say: "Praise be to Allah, who has not taken a child"} the verse: the Jews and the Christians said, Allah has taken a child, and the Arabs said, "Here we are at Your service, here we are, You have no partner", except a partner that is Yours, whom You own along with what he owns. And the Sabians and the Magians said, were it not for the allies of Allah, He would be lowly. So Allah revealed this verse: {And say: "Praise be to Allah, who has not taken a child, nor has He a partner in dominion, nor has He a protector out of weakness," and magnify Him with great magnification}.

He also said: [chain] Bishr told us, [Yazid told us], Sa'id told us, from Qatadah: it was mentioned to us that the Prophet ﷺ used to teach his household this verse, {And say: "Praise be to Allah, who has not taken a child, nor has He a partner in dominion, nor has He a protector out of weakness," and magnify Him with great magnification}, both the young and the old of his household.

I say: it has come in a hadith that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ named it the verse of might (ayat al-izz), and in some reports: it has never been recited in a house on a night without that house being protected from theft or affliction. And Allah knows best.

Al-Hafiz Abu Ya'la said: [chain] Bishr ibn Sayhan al-Basri told us, Harb ibn Maymun told us, Musa ibn Ubaydah al-Rabadhi told us, from Muhammad ibn Ka'b al-Qurazi, from Abu Hurayrah, who said: I went out, I and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, my hand in his hand, and he came upon a man of shabby appearance, and said: "O so-and-so, what has brought you to what I see?" He said: sickness and hardship, O Messenger of Allah. He said: "Shall I not teach you words that will remove sickness and hardship from you?" He said: yes. He said: it would not please me more if I had witnessed Badr or Uhud with you. He said: so the Messenger of Allah ﷺ laughed and said: "Can the people of Badr and the people of Uhud attain what the contented poor person attains?" He said: so Abu Hurayrah said: O Messenger of Allah, teach me too. He said: so say, O Abu Hurayrah: "I have placed my trust in the Living One who does not die. Praise be to Allah, who has not taken a child, nor has He a partner in dominion, nor has He a protector out of weakness, and magnify Him with great magnification." He said: so the Messenger of Allah later came to me and my condition had become good, and he said to me: "What has happened?" He said: I said: I have not ceased saying the words which you taught me.

Its chain of transmission is weak, and its text contains something objectionable (nakarah). And Allah knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: قُلْ يَا مُحَمَّدُ، لِهَؤُلَاءِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ الْمُنْكِرِينَ صِفَةَ الرَّحْمَةِ لِلَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، الْمَانِعِينَ مِنْ تَسْمِيَتِهِ بِالرَّحْمَنِ: ﴿ادْعُوا اللَّهَ أَوِ ادْعُوا الرَّحْمَنَ أَيًّا مَا تَدْعُوا فَلَهُ الأسْمَاءُ الْحُسْنَى﴾ أَيْ: لَا فَرْقَ بَيْنَ دُعَائِكُمْ لَهُ بِاسْمِ "اللَّهِ" أَوْ بِاسْمِ " الرَّحْمَنِ "، فَإِنَّهُ ذُو الْأَسْمَاءِ الْحُسْنَى، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿هُوَ اللَّهُ الَّذِي لَا إِلَهَ إِلا هُوَ عَالِمُ الْغَيْبِ وَالشَّهَادَةِ هُوَ الرَّحْمَنُ الرَّحِيمُ﴾ إِلَى أَنْ قَالَ: ﴿لَهُ الأسْمَاءُ الْحُسْنَى يُسَبِّحُ لَهُ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ وَهُوَ الْعَزِيزُ الْحَكِيمُ﴾ [الْحَشْرِ: ٢٢ -٢٤] .

وَقَدْ رَوَى مَكْحُولٌ أَنَّ رَجُلًا مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ سَمِعَ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ وَهُوَ يَقُولُ فِي سُجُودِهِ: "يَا رَحْمَنُ يَا رَحِيمُ"، فَقَالَ: إِنَّهُ يَزْعُمُ أَنَّهُ يَدْعُو وَاحِدًا، وَهُوَ يَدْعُو اثْنَيْنِ. فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ. وَكَذَا رُوِيَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، رَوَاهُمَا ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلا تَجْهَرْ بِصَلاتِكَ﴾ الْآيَةَ، قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا هُشَيْم، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو بِشْرٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: نَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ وَهُوَ مُتَوَارٍ بِمَكَّةَ ﴿وَلا تَجْهَرْ بِصَلاتِكَ وَلا تُخَافِتْ بِهَا [وَابْتَغِ بَيْنَ ذَلِكَ سَبِيلا] ﴾ قَالَ: كَانَ إِذَا صَلَّى بِأَصْحَابِهِ رَفَعَ صَوْتَهُ بِالْقُرْآنِ، فَلَمَّا سَمِعَ ذَلِكَ الْمُشْرِكُونَ سَبُّوا الْقُرْآنَ، وَسَبُّوا مَنْ أَنْزَلَهُ، وَمَنْ جَاءَ بِهِ. قَالَ: فَقَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى لِنَبِيِّهِ ﷺ: ﴿وَلا تَجْهَرْ بِصَلاتِكَ﴾ أَيْ: بِقِرَاءَتِكَ فيسمع المشركون فيسبوا القرآن ﴿وَلا تُخَافِتْ بِهَا﴾ عَنْ أَصْحَابِكَ فَلَا تُسْمِعُهُمُ الْقُرْآنَ حَتَّى يَأْخُذُوهُ عَنْكَ ﴿وَابْتَغِ بَيْنَ ذَلِكَ سَبِيلا﴾ .

أَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي بِشْرٍ جَعْفَرِ بْنِ إِيَاسٍ، بِهِ وَكَذَا رَوَى الضَّحَّاكُ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَزَادَ: "فَلَمَّا هَاجَرَ إِلَى الْمَدِينَةِ، سَقَطَ ذَلِكَ، يَفْعَلُ أَيَّ ذَلِكَ شَاءَ" .

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ إِسْحَاقَ: حَدَّثَنِي دَاوُدَ بْنِ الْحُصَيْنِ، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِذَا جَهَرَ بِالْقُرْآنِ وَهُوَ يُصَلِّي، تَفَرَّقُوا عَنْهُ وَأَبَوْا أَنْ يَسْمَعُوا مِنْهُ، فَكَانَ الرَّجُلُ إِذَا أَرَادَ أَنْ يَسْتَمِعَ مِنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ بَعْضَ مَا يَتْلُو وَهُوَ يُصَلِّي، اسْتَرَقَ السَّمْعَ دُونَهُمْ فَرَقًا مِنْهُمْ، فَإِنْ رَأَى أَنَّهُمْ قَدْ عَرَفُوا أَنَّهُ يَسْتَمِعُ ، ذَهَبَ خَشْيَةَ أَذَاهُمْ فَلَمْ يَسْتَمِعْ ، فَإِنْ خَفَضَ صَوْتَهُ ﷺ لَمْ يَسْتَمِعِ الَّذِينَ يَسْتَمِعُونَ مِنْ قِرَاءَتِهِ شَيْئًا، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ ﴿وَلا تَجْهَرْ بِصَلاتِكَ﴾ فَيَتَفَرَّقُوا عَنْكَ ﴿وَلا تُخَافِتْ بِهَا﴾ فَلَا تُسمع مَنْ أَرَادَ أَنْ يَسْمَعَهَا مِمَّنْ يَسْتَرِقُ ذَلِكَ دُونَهُمْ، لَعَلَّهُ يَرْعَوِي إِلَى بَعْضِ مَا يَسْمَعُ، فَيَنْتَفِعَ بِهِ ﴿وَابْتَغِ بَيْنَ ذَلِكَ سَبِيلا﴾

وَهَكَذَا قَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ، وَالْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ، وَقَتَادَةُ: نَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ فِي الْقِرَاءَةِ فِي الصَّلَاةِ.

وَقَالَ شُعْبَةُ عَنْ أَشْعَثَ بْنِ أَبِي سُلَيْمٍ عَنِ الْأَسْوَدِ بْنِ هِلَالٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ: لَمْ يُخافتْ بِهَا مَنْ أَسْمَعَ أُذُنَيْهِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا يَعْقُوبُ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ عُلَيَّة، عَنْ سَلَمَةُ بْنُ عَلْقَمَةَ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ سِيرِينَ قَالَ: نُبِّئْتُ أَنَّ أَبَا بَكْرٍ كَانَ إِذَا صَلَّى فَقَرَأَ خَفَضَ صَوْتَهُ، وَأَنَّ عُمَرَ كَانَ يَرْفَعُ صَوْتَهُ، فَقِيلَ لِأَبِي بَكْرٍ: لِمَ تَصْنَعُ هَذَا؟ قَالَ: أُنَاجِي رَبِّي، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، وَقَدْ عَلِمَ حَاجَتِي. فَقِيلَ: أَحْسَنْتَ. وَقِيلَ لِعُمَرَ: لِمَ تَصْنَعُ هَذَا؟ قَالَ: أَطْرُدُ الشَّيْطَانَ، وَأُوقِظُ الوَسْنَان. قِيلَ أَحْسَنْتَ. فَلَمَّا نَزَلَتْ: ﴿وَلا تَجْهَرْ بِصَلاتِكَ وَلا تُخَافِتْ بِهَا وَابْتَغِ بَيْنَ ذَلِكَ سَبِيلا﴾ قِيلَ لِأَبِي بَكْرٍ: ارْفَعْ شَيْئًا، وَقِيلَ لِعُمَرَ: اخْفِضْ شَيْئًا .

وَقَالَ أَشْعَثَ بْنِ سَوَّار، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: نَزَلَتْ فِي الدُّعَاءِ. وَهَكَذَا رَوَى الثَّوْرِيُّ، وَمَالِكٌ، عَنْ هِشَامِ بْنِ عُرْوَةَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ: نَزَلَتْ فِي الدُّعَاءِ. وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَأَبُو عِياض، وَمَكْحُولٌ، وَعُرْوَةُ بْنُ الزُّبَيْرِ.

وَقَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ عَنْ [ابْنِ] عَيَّاشٍ الْعَامِرِيِّ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ شَدَّادٍ قَالَ: كَانَ أَعْرَابٌ مِنْ بَنِي تَمِيمٍ إِذَا سَلَّمَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ قَالُوا: اللَّهُمَّ ارْزُقْنَا إِبِلًا وَوَلَدًا. قَالَ: فَنَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ: ﴿وَلا تَجْهَرْ بِصَلاتِكَ وَلا تُخَافِتْ بِهَا﴾

قَوْلٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو السَّائِبِ، حَدَّثَنَا حَفْصُ بْنُ غِيَاثٍ، عَنْ هِشَامِ بْنِ عُرْوَةَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، نَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ فِي التَّشَهُّدِ: ﴿وَلا تَجْهَرْ بِصَلاتِكَ وَلا تُخَافِتْ بِهَا﴾

وَبِهِ قَالَ حَفْصٌ، عَنْ أَشْعَثَ بْنِ سَوَّارٍ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ سِيرِينَ، مِثْلَهُ.

قَوْلٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلا تَجْهَرْ بِصَلاتِكَ وَلا تُخَافِتْ بِهَا﴾ قَالَ: لَا تُصَلِّ مُرَاءَاةَ النَّاسِ، وَلَا تَدَعَهَا مَخَافَةَ النَّاسِ. وَقَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ مَنْصُورٍ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ الْبَصْرِيِّ: ﴿وَلا تَجْهَرْ بِصَلاتِكَ وَلا تُخَافِتْ بِهَا﴾ قَالَ: لَا تُحْسِنْ عَلَانِيَتَهَا وَتُسِيءَ سَرِيرَتَهَا. وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، عَنْ مَعْمَرٍ، عَنْ الْحَسَنِ، بِهِ. وهُشَيْم، عَنْ عَوْفٍ، عَنْهُ بِهِ. وَسَعِيدٌ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنْهُ كَذَلِكَ.

قَوْلٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَابْتَغِ بَيْنَ ذَلِكَ سَبِيلا﴾ قَالَ: أَهْلُ الْكِتَابِ يُخَافِتُونَ، ثُمَّ يَجْهَرُ أَحَدُهُمْ بِالْحَرْفِ فَيَصِيحُ بِهِ، وَيَصِيحُونَ هُمْ بِهِ وَرَاءَهُ، فَنَهَاهُ أَنْ يَصِيحَ كَمَا يَصِيحُ هَؤُلَاءِ، وَأَنْ يُخَافِتَ كَمَا يُخَافِتُ الْقَوْمُ، ثُمَّ كَانَ السَّبِيلُ الَّذِي بَيْنَ ذَلِكَ، الَّذِي سَنَّ لَهُ جِبْرِيلُ مِنَ الصَّلَاةِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَقُلِ الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ الَّذِي لَمْ يَتَّخِذْ وَلَدًا﴾ لَمَّا أَثْبَتَ تَعَالَى لِنَفْسِهِ الْكَرِيمَةِ الْأَسْمَاءَ الْحُسْنَى، نَزَّهَ نَفْسَهُ عَنِ النَّقَائِصِ فَقَالَ: ﴿وَقُلِ الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ الَّذِي لَمْ يَتَّخِذْ وَلَدًا وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ شَرِيكٌ فِي الْمُلْكِ﴾ بَلْ هُوَ اللَّهُ الْأَحَدُ الصَّمَدُ، الَّذِي لَمْ يَلِدْ وَلَمْ يُولَدْ، وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ كُفُوًا أَحَدٌ.

﴿وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ وَلِيٌّ مِنَ الذُّلِّ﴾ أَيْ: لَيْسَ بِذَلِيلٍ فَيَحْتَاجَ أَنْ يَكُونَ لَهُ وَلِيٌّ أَوْ وَزِيرٌ أَوْ مُشِيرٌ، بَلْ هُوَ تَعَالَى [شَأْنُهُ] خَالِقُ الْأَشْيَاءِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، وَمُقَدِّرُهَا وَمُدَبِّرُهَا بِمَشِيئَتِهِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ وَلِيٌّ مِنَ الذُّلِّ﴾ لَمْ يُحَالِفْ أَحَدًا وَلَا يَبْتَغِي نَصْرَ أَحَدٍ.

﴿وَكَبِّرْهُ تَكْبِيرًا﴾ أَيْ: عظِّمه وأَجِلَّه عَمَّا يَقُولُ الظَّالِمُونَ الْمُعْتَدُونَ عُلُوًّا كَبِيرًا.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي يُونُسُ، أَنْبَأَنَا ابْنُ وَهْبٍ، أَخْبَرَنِي أَبُو صَخْرٍ، عَنِ الْقُرَظِيِّ أَنَّهُ كَانَ يَقُولُ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿وَقُلِ الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ الَّذِي لَمْ يَتَّخِذْ وَلَدًا﴾ الْآيَةَ، قَالَ: إِنَّ الْيَهُودَ وَالنَّصَارَى قَالُوا: اتَّخَذَ اللَّهُ وَلَدًا، وَقَالَ الْعَرَبُ: [لَبَّيْكَ] لَبَّيْكَ، لَا شَرِيكَ لَكَ؛ إِلَّا شَرِيكًا هُوَ لَكَ، تَمْلِكُهُ وَمَا مَلَكَ. وَقَالَ الصَّابِئُونَ وَالْمَجُوسُ: لَوْلَا أَوْلِيَاءُ اللَّهِ لَذَلَّ. فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿وَقُلِ الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ الَّذِي لَمْ يَتَّخِذْ وَلَدًا وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ شَرِيكٌ فِي الْمُلْكِ وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ وَلِيٌّ مِنَ الذُّلِّ وَكَبِّرْهُ تَكْبِيرًا﴾

وَقَالَ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا بِشْرٌ، [حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ] حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدٌ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ: ذُكِرَ لَنَا أَنَّ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ كَانَ يُعَلِّمُ أَهْلَهُ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ ﴿وَقُلِ الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ الَّذِي لَمْ يَتَّخِذْ وَلَدًا وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ شَرِيكٌ فِي الْمُلْكِ وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ وَلِيٌّ مِنَ الذُّلِّ وَكَبِّرْهُ تَكْبِيرًا﴾ الصَّغِيرَ مِنْ أَهْلِهِ وَالْكَبِيرَ.

قُلْتُ: وَقَدْ جَاءَ فِي حَدِيثٍ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ سَمَّاهَا آيَةَ الْعِزِّ وَفِي بَعْضِ الْآثَارِ: أَنَّهَا مَا قُرِئَتْ فِي بَيْتٍ فِي لَيْلَةٍ فَيُصِيبَهُ سَرَقٌ أَوْ آفَةٌ. وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو يَعْلَى: حَدَّثَنَا بِشْرُ بْنُ سَيْحَانَ الْبَصْرِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا حرب بن ميمون، حدثنا موسى ابن عُبَيْدَةَ الرَّبَذي، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ كَعْبٍ القُرَظي، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: خَرَجْتُ أَنَا وَرَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَيَدِي فِي يَدِهِ، فَأَتَى عَلَى رَجُلٍ رَثِّ الْهَيْئَةِ، فَقَالَ: "أَيْ فُلَانُ، مَا بَلَغَ بِكَ مَا أَرَى؟ ". قَالَ: السَّقَمُ وَالضُّرُّ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ. قَالَ: "أَلَّا أُعَلِّمُكَ كَلِمَاتٍ تُذْهِبُ عَنْكَ السَّقَمَ وَالضُّرَّ؟ ". قَالَ: لَا قَالَ: مَا يَسُرُّنِي بِهَا أَنْ شَهِدْتُ مَعَكَ بَدْرًا أَوْ أَحَدًا. قَالَ: فَضَحِكَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ وقال: "وَهَلْ يُدْرِكُ أَهْلُ بَدْرٍ وَأَهْلُ أُحُدٍ مَا يُدْرِكُ الْفَقِيرُ الْقَانِعُ؟ ". قَالَ: فَقَالَ أَبُو هُرَيْرَةَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِيَّايَ فَعَلِّمْنِي قَالَ: فَقُلْ يَا أَبَا هُرَيْرَةَ: "تَوَكَّلْتُ عَلَى الْحَيِّ الَّذِي لَا يَمُوتُ، الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ الَّذِي لَمْ يَتَّخِذْ وَلَدًا، وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ شَرِيكٌ فِي الْمُلْكِ، وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ وَلِيٌّ مِنَ الذُّلِّ، وَكَبِّرْهُ تَكْبِيرًا". قَالَ: فَأَتَى عَلَيَّ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ وَقَدْ حَسُنَت حَالِي، قَالَ: فَقَالَ لِي: "مَهْيم". قَالَ: قُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، لَمْ أَزَلْ أَقُولُ الْكَلِمَاتِ الَّتِي عَلَّمْتَنِي .

إِسْنَادُهُ ضَعِيفٌ وَفِي مَتْنِهِ نكارة. [والله أعلم] .

---
